National Army Revolutionary Memorial

(Nanjing) October 23rd is the National Army Revolutionary Memorial Day. Recalling this day in the 13th year of the Republic of China, Feng Yuxiang and Hu Jingyi used their troops in the former capital to drive out the president Cao Kun, who was elected through bribery, and implemented the National Revolution, which was a great honor in history. Now, the graves of the two deceased pioneers, Hu and Sun, have been overgrown with trees, and comrades who participated in the National Army Revolution, such as Feng Yuxiang, Zhang Ji, Yu Youren, Ding Weifen, Wang Faqin, Lu Zhonglin, Zhang Fang, Zhang Qun, Jiao Yitang, Yang Hucheng, Wang Yongbin, etc., are building a ancestral hall for Duke Hu in Zhengzhou and have established a committee to handle the matter, in order to show the intention of commemorating the martyrs for thousands of years. The association has notified that the National Army Revolutionary Memorial and the completion ceremony of the Duke Hu Ancestral Hall will be held simultaneously in Beijing, Zhengzhou, and other places on October 23rd. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Subsidizes Tax Revenue Methods

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance previously stipulated that 30% of the stamp tax revenue of each province should be allocated for subsidies, because the income of each province would inevitably be in deficit due to the abolition of harsh and miscellaneous taxes. Now, in order to simplify the remittance procedures for this subsidy tax, special methods have been formulated and are being promoted in the six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Shandong, and Hubei. Separate letters have been sent to the Central Bank, the six provincial governments, and the tax supervision committees of the six provinces for investigation and handling. The content of the method is as follows: the post offices in the six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Shandong, and Henan will deposit 30% of the stamp tax revenue collected by each county into the branches of the Central Bank in each province on a monthly basis, which will be collected as an account of the Ministry of Finance. At the same time, it will be reported to the Tax Administration and the provincial governments, and the provincial governments will assess the situation of the abolition of harsh and miscellaneous taxes in each county according to the 30% number of tax revenue, determine the number of allocations for each county, and consult with the tax supervision committees of each province to create a detailed list and send it to the Ministry of Finance. Then the Ministry of Finance will send a letter to the Central Bank to transfer the 30% stamp tax revenue stored by the Ministry of Finance to the branches of each province according to the number of items on the list, and directly remit it to the county governments of each province for collection, and obtain the official receipts from the county governments and send them to the Ministry. If the county governments have regular taxes to be paid to the provincial treasury, they may use the above funds to offset them. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Provinces and Cities Levying Labor Service, Executive Yuan Orders Plans to Be Submitted for Approval

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan's outline of twelve articles on the method of levying labor service orders the provincial and municipal governments to quickly draft a complete labor service plan in accordance with the outline and submit it for approval. The purpose of labor service is mainly for projects such as self-defense, road construction, water conservancy, and afforestation. All able-bodied men between the ages of eighteen and forty-five must serve three to five days of labor service each year, but those who are disabled and unable to work are exempt from service. Commentary

Yet Another Manifestation of the Power of Unity

— Du

Han Fuju, the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, rushed to Zhejiang a few days ago to have a formal meeting with President Jiang of the Executive Yuan. At the same time, Xu Yongchang, the Qingxiang Superintendent of Shanxi, Yang Hucheng, the Pacification Commissioner of Shaanxi Province, and Ge Dingyuan, the Secretary-General of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, also traveled to Hangzhou without prior arrangement. Although the duties of these individuals were officially different, some sought instructions on bandit suppression due to their responsibilities, while others reported on local political situations as part of their duties. In any case, at a time when the situation in North China is extremely tense, the fact that these important responsible individuals were able to meet on a timely basis is enough to attract the attention of ordinary people. The impact should not be underestimated. After waiting eagerly, we are happy to extend our very warm sympathy.

While Zhang Qun's trip to Sichuan is underway to adjust diplomatic relations, the alarms on the eastern border of Suiyuan are frequent, and the plotting of the unprincipled is becoming increasingly urgent. The background is not difficult to imagine. We also know that the desires of our neighbors are endless and insatiable. Unless we "threaten with threats," it will be impossible to curb their ambitions even by a slim chance. However, it is still believed that with sincere interactions between the two parties and the attention of the international community, even those with excessive greed will not be without regard for justice. Therefore, even if the situation in eastern Suiyuan is extremely complicated today, the bandit crowds who come out to disturb the border still belong to the unfilial elements in the country. Knowing that there are puppeteers behind the scenes, we know that there are others who are pulling the strings. Judging from their chaotic forces, it is not difficult to put them down. If the people of the country can all examine their behavior and encourage themselves with the concept of the nation, and not easily be used by others, then the current tenuous connection may not be broken suddenly. We fear that shameless traitors are willing to be accomplices, using their old tricks of infiltration and resorting to their tricks of coercion, so that the local authorities are gradually trapped in their trap. This is also what we deeply deplore. This decision of Han, Xu, and others to go south together to have frank meetings with the central authorities can at least dispel the anxieties that have been lingering in our hearts for a long time.

We firmly believe that only by concentrating the strength of the whole country can we resist foreign aggression and save the nation. We also firmly believe that under the principle of resisting foreign aggression and saving the nation, there is nothing that cannot bring the whole country to unity. Therefore, unity is the only important task today. And the grand plan after unity should be the steps that should be determined urgently at present. The fact that the affairs of Guangdong and Guangxi, which were not easy to sort out, were resolved quickly in a short period of time is because of the requirements of the times, and there must be a united situation. The fact that the senior officials in North China do not often meet on weekdays and there are inevitably differences in opinion can now calmly express their feelings to each other during the cup-passing, which can be said to be yet another manifestation of the power of unity. Here, we can more firmly believe that under the formation of united forces, any national crisis cannot be overcome. At the same time, we can also understand that those who threaten us with threats are not precisely the driving force behind the promotion of unity in our country?

Kirkpatrick Appointed British Representative to China: Credit Lending Plan Will Be Strictly Based on Commerce

(London) Mr. Kirkpatrick, a Conservative Member of the British Parliament, has been appointed as the representative of the Export Credits Guarantee Department to China, responsible for studying various proposals under the new Sino-British export credit lending plan. It is reported that Mr. Kirkpatrick will work jointly with the British government trade representative originally stationed in China. Mr. Kirkpatrick, who is currently 58 years old, previously engaged in the import business of British textiles in Delhi, India, for many years. He also represented Samuel & Co. in Japan, the East Asia Telephone Company in Hong Kong, and London bankers in Chile. In addition, he also traveled to Athens for financial matters. Mr. Nicholson, the manager of the Export Credits Guarantee Department, told a Reuters reporter today that "We have received many proposals requiring guarantees, all advocating that British manufacturers should make good use of the opportunities in China. However, due to the rapid changes in the current situation in China, it is particularly difficult to assess the degree of risk in credit lending. The newly appointed representative to China, Mr. Kirkpatrick, will be in charge of all financial and economic proposals. The implementation of this plan will be strictly based on commerce and will not provide any subsidies to British trade." Mr. Nicholson also denied the rumors of British loans to China, continuing, "The original intention of appointing Mr. Kirkpatrick as the representative to China is only to enable domestic manufacturers to occupy a more important position in China's trade, because China has seen amazing developments in industry over the past two years, and everything is now more stable than before. We are prepared to take on some of the responsibility for the risks. China's great demand for factory machinery is mostly supplied by foreign countries." At the end of his conversation, Mr. Nicholson solemnly declared that arms manufacturers would not be allowed to participate in this credit lending plan. (Reuters, 19th)

Ciano Questions Rome: Italy and Germany Seek Cooperation, Discuss Three Matters, Decide on Unified Steps: Relationship Between the Two Dictatorial Countries Will Likely Be Closer

(Rome) Count Ciano, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, was originally scheduled to fly to Berlin tomorrow, but he has advanced the trip to this afternoon, traveling to Germany with the German Ambassador, Mr. Hassel. He is expected to stay in Berlin for three days and then go to Berchtesgaden to meet with the German leader, Hitler, and stay for two days. Informed sources recently announced that Foreign Minister Ciano's trip may bring back Germany's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia. (Havas, 19th)

(Rome) Although the official mission of the Foreign Minister's trip has not been announced, responsible sources claim that the Foreign Minister and the German authorities do not intend to negotiate any special issues, but will discuss the following three matters with the German leader Hitler and Foreign Minister Neurath: (1) Preparations for the Vienna Conference of the diplomatic authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary (this conference is scheduled to begin on November 9); (2) The attitudes that Germany and Italy should take regarding the future Locarno Treaty after Belgium restores its neutral status; (3) The issue of communism in Europe, among which the third is considered the most important. Observers say that the mutual understanding between Germany and Italy will be highlighted by Ciano's trip. Although Germany and Italy have not established a formal agreement or signed a treaty of alliance, the diplomatic policies pursued by both sides are consistent. In addition, there is another purpose, which is to promote bilateral economic relations, as seen by the recent visits of many German industrial leaders to northern Italy and Rome. (Havas, 19th)

(Paris) Italian Foreign Minister Ciano is scheduled to depart for Berlin tomorrow. The renowned journalist Bertina recently published an article in the Echo de Paris, commenting, "The most important aspect of the international diplomatic situation this week will be Ciano's trip. It is difficult for the foreign policies of Italy's fascist government and Germany's National Socialist government to achieve complete harmony. Therefore, the mission of Ciano's trip is to find a way for Italy and Germany to cooperate, so that the two countries can share common interests in the short term. However, in order to prevent the progress of National Socialist Pan-Germanism, the Italian government cannot completely break away from Britain and France. But in order to expand its position in the Mediterranean and Africa, it must feign intimacy with Germany to control Britain and France. This is the subtle use of Italian foreign policy. In short, the purpose of Ciano's trip is to ensure that Germany promises to take consistent steps with Italy on all important issues." (Havas, 19th)

(Rome) Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano will soon go to Berlin to visit German Foreign Minister Neurath and exchange views with German leader Hitler. Messengers between Germany and Italy are constantly traveling back and forth. Mr. Ciano's trip is only one of them. General Milch, a senior official of the German Air Ministry, recently visited General Val, a senior official of the Italian Air Force. He departed today after completing his official duties. As soon as Mr. Milch left, General Himmler, the German Chief of Police, arrived to visit Mr. Bocchini, the head of the Italian secret political police. (Reuters, 19th)

Belgian Government to Announce New National Defense Plan: To Resist Any German Aggression: Germany Increases Defense on the Left Bank of the Rhine

(Paris) According to reliable sources today, the Belgian government will announce a new national defense plan to resist any German aggression. At the same time, it is understood that the Belgian government will allow France to extend the Maginot Line to the coast. This new Belgian policy is expected to be announced at a special session of parliament next week. (National Telegram, 19th)

(Strasbourg, France) According to informed sources, the German General Staff is actively increasing its defensive forces on the left bank of the Rhine, especially in the Palatinate region. A newly formed army division, numbered the 36th Division, is stationed in the area. It can be seen that the German active army has at least twelve corps, each divided into three divisions. In addition, troops have also been transferred from East Prussia to the Rhine border. (Havas, 19th)

Belgium's Policy: Upholding the Principle of Collective Mutual Assistance: Drawing Lessons from Abyssinia's Fate

Brussels: Foreign Minister Spaak recently delivered a speech at the Socialist Federation of the Municipality, stating that Belgium should continue to adhere to the principles of collective security and mutual assistance, but Belgium cannot accept using this principle as the sole basis for its foreign policy. "Abyssinia mistakenly believed that its national defense policy, if based on a collective security system, could rest easy. But what was the result?" (Havas, 18th)

Romania: Respecting Alliances: Guaranteeing Border Security

Romanian Capital: Today is the second anniversary of the merger of the Farmers' Party of Outer Transylvania into the National Farmers' Party. The National Farmers' Party held a large gathering to celebrate. The party's secretary-general, Magano, delivered a speech, stating, "The security of Romania's borders is based on the alliance system. The alliance system is the alliance established between our country and France, Poland, the Little Entente, and the Balkan Entente countries, and it must not be weakened. We also hope that a regional security pact can be established." (Havas, 18th)

Large Political Gathering in Vienna: Schuschnigg's Speech: Expounding the Advantages of Constitutional Policies: The Audience is Particularly Indifferent

(Vienna) Austrian Chancellor Dr. Schuschnigg announced yesterday that the legitimist movement was legal and foreshadowed a referendum on the future political system of Austria. The whole of Europe was surprised. However, when he spoke to Austria's largest political gathering in history in Schwechat today, the audience was particularly indifferent. The gathering was carefully prepared and announced in advance. 150,000 people from Lower Austria were transported to the meeting free of charge by train. The authorities prepared a rich breakfast to await the crowds attending the meeting and gave each person a ticket, which could be used to watch a football game or a drama movie. No fewer than 390,000 people participated in the meeting. Dr. Schuschnigg spoke from a newly built 70-foot-high platform, trying to explain the advantages of his "guild" constitutional policy, but failed to arouse enthusiastic welcome from the audience. Dr. Schuschnigg then promised to reform Austrian society, reduce coal prices, and provide school children with free milk from the state, but the crowd remained silent and unmoved. (Reuters, 18th)

Dutch Airlines: Purchasing Giant Aircraft: Planning to Cross the North Atlantic: Make Non-Stop Flights

The Hague: Dutch Airlines has recently planned a non-stop flight from New York to Amsterdam, Netherlands. No one has ever flown directly between these two places. It is planned to use the latest "Flying Hotel" giant aircraft for this purpose. The company has recently purchased several of these aircraft for the Amsterdam-Batavia route. (Reuters, 19th)

Prime Minister Blum Calls On the French Popular Front to Unite: Support the Government to Realize the Political Program: Do Not Give Enemy Parties a Chance to Exploit

Orléans, France: Prime Minister Blum delivered an important political speech at the joint banquet of the Radical Socialist Party of the Loiret Province tonight. The speech lasted an hour. The Prime Minister first described the French political situation before the general election in May of this year, then analyzed the situation since the establishment of the Popular Front government for four and a half months, as well as the inappropriate situation caused by social agitation. Finally, he presented an outline of the actions to be taken in the future. The speech was very long. A summary is as follows:

The Prime Minister said, "Opinions may differ on whether we like or dislike what we have done, but we have already done something. This cannot be denied by any honest gentleman. I would now like to raise a question that urgently needs to be resolved: Should we continue to work? Will we still receive the support of the original majority in Parliament? Will we still be supported by the original political and social groups? If we put this question to the people for judgment, the answer will be undoubtedly no, because the ideals of the Popular Front have not been damaged in the slightest since last June, and the people's enthusiasm for the Popular Front has not diminished in the slightest. If so, how can we re-divide at this time? Although the formation of the Popular Front was obtained with the permission of the people, some people still express doubts about the internal structure and duration of the Popular Front. This has caused unrest among our friendly parties, and our enemy parties want to take the opportunity to attack the Communist Party. Regarding these doubts, I dare to answer that if a party withdraws from the Popular Front and no longer trusts the government, the only result will be to dissolve the House of Representatives and hold a re-election to solicit public opinion."

The Prime Minister then recounted the history of the formation of the Popular Front, saying, "The Popular Front was born on the day of the February 6, 1934, Paris riots. Fascist groups were the parents who gave birth to the Popular Front. At that time, the power of fascist groups was quite rampant. Therefore, political parties and groups willing to protect democracy and freedom were forced to unite. In any period of French history, if the harmonious cooperation of the workers and peasants has not been obtained, the republican system has not been able to obtain effective protection. As for the issue that most Radical Party members are worried about, it is the issue of legal order, because the waves of labor unrest are endless, and workers often occupy factories. This is what worries the Radical Party the most. I think that in order to save the republican system, the first thing is to continue to maintain legal order. Constant social disputes will inevitably make the bourgeoisie and farmers fear. If the Popular Front government cannot restore true order in spirit and in practice, it will become weak and powerless." Mr. Blum added, "If the Communist Party withdraws from the Popular Front, then those reactionaries know that the Socialist Party is also Marxist, and they will inevitably take a further step to force the Socialist Party to withdraw from the Popular Front. If so, then only you (referring to the Radical Party) will bear the brunt of the conflict."

At this point, Mr. Blum described the general situation in France and Europe, saying, "Two years ago, Europe was divided into two major camps: democratic politics and fascism. Now it is not. Some people are now trying to divide Europe into two major camps: dictatorial politics and communism. In France, those who wish to maintain order no longer think of dictatorship. Any party of the Popular Front has only one purpose: to continue to seek progress within the scope of order and democracy. To guarantee the development of democratic politics and to seek social democratization through political democratization is nothing more than expanding the principles of the French Revolution of 1789 on the scale of modern society. Within the Popular Front, each party should maintain the right to autonomy, but this autonomy should be used to make a joint effort by each party. Although these two things seem to be contradictory, they are actually complementary." In conclusion, he said, "We should seek thorough reforms, but this reform does not conflict with the property system. We aim to create a new society, but the method we use is only to improve the existing society." After Mr. Blum finished his speech, the whole room applauded for a long time. Then, they sang the Marseillaise and the Internationale together and announced the end of the meeting. (Havas, 18th)

(London) It was learned here today that British bombers have invented the use of a rotating machine gun, the gun mount rotating like those equipped on warships. All equipment is powered by machinery. (National Telegram, 19th)

China's Construction: Great Progress: Smuggling Affects Trade in Various Countries: US Department of Commerce Releases Investigation Report

(Washington) The Department of Commerce released a world business survey report today, stating that China has made rapid progress domestically since the unification was completed in September. However, China's foreign relations have failed to stabilize, making it impossible for business to be optimistic. Japan's Mandated Islands: Annual Report: Denying Military Equipment

(Geneva) Japan submitted an annual report on the mandated islands to the League of Nations today, stating that Japan has unswervingly complied with the League of Nations' prohibition on turning the mandated islands in the South Pacific into military bases. Since the Japanese government established the South Seas Bureau in 1932, the troops stationed on the islands have gradually withdrawn, and the local indigenous people have not engaged in military training. The development of port services on the islands is purely commercial. Japan also allowed 58 foreigners to visit the islands in 1935, including seven Americans. No defense-style naval base has been built on the islands. The report's wording is mild. It is generally believed to be a gesture of goodwill towards Britain and the United States. (National Telegram, 19th)

Western Rebel Army Continues to Occupy Important Towns: The Capital's Position Becomes More Precarious: The Vanguard is Only Sixteen Miles Away: Cannon Fire Can Be Heard Clearly

Talavera: It is heard that the rebel army has occupied Robledo de Chavela, 26 miles northwest of Madrid. This is the last major defense line of the Escorial Palace, built by King Philip II to commemorate the victory over the French army at the Battle of Saint-Quentin on Saint Lawrence Day (August 10) in 1557. It is expected that the fall of the palace will have a great impact on morale. The rebel army, which captured the town of Illescas on the Madrid-Toledo road yesterday, asked its commander this morning to allow it to attack Madrid immediately, but the rebel commander did not approve it because the entire attack plan had to be carefully coordinated and carried out. The northwest of Madrid is mountainous, so the rebel army's mechanized forces have almost no use, resulting in the inability to advance as quickly as on the southern plains of the capital. The rebel army is only sixteen miles away from the capital in several places, so the sound of its cannon fire can be heard clearly in the suburbs of the capital. It is now believed that the fall of the important railway junction of Castillejo, on the Madrid-Valencia railway, has shaken the morale of the militia. Civil servants and employees of various businesses are now helping to dig trenches and build defensive works around the capital. They are very diligent. The rebel army is now eager to attack quickly, because snow has already fallen in the mountains. The Moorish troops are quite intolerant of the cold. Each person wears three or four layers of outerwear, otherwise they cannot stand on their own. (Reuters, 19th)

Talavera: Today, a rebel army column has occupied the town of Illescas, 24 miles from the capital on the Madrid-Toledo road, so the fall of Madrid is getting closer and closer. This town is a key point in the defense of the capital. The militia defending the town did not make a fierce resistance. Government troops are still holding several places in the mountains between Madrid and Escorial, but it seems that there is a risk of being cut off by the rebel army advancing from the southwest. (Reuters, 18th)

Madrid: A special report from our reporter states that the National Army, led by Colonel Barron, engaged in a fierce battle with a battalion of shock troops belonging to the government army on the south side of the capital yesterday. The government army was defeated and retreated, leaving behind more than 200 bodies. The retreat was still in good order. The National Army immediately attacked and entered the city of Illescas (37 kilometers south of the capital). Four large three-engine aircraft belonging to the government army flew over the city. Two of them were shot down by fighter planes belonging to the National Army, and the remaining two escaped. In addition, a cavalry team led by Colonel Monasterio of the National Army advanced along the road from Toledo to the capital and has arrived at a certain place 14 kilometers from Aranjuez. (Havas, 19th)

Talavera: The rebel air force is very superior. Since the siege of Oviedo in northern Spain was lifted, it has almost surpassed the government air force, because the entire rebel air force can now be concentrated to attack the defenders of Madrid. At the same time, the Moorish troops and foreign troops who occupied Oviedo have formed two major columns and will soon depart to the provinces of Gijón and Santander on the coast of the Bay of Biscay to eliminate the government troops in the area. Also, the shock troops, volunteers, and foreign troops of the rebel army have victoriously entered the city of Oviedo yesterday and met with the besieged garrison there. (Reuters, 19th)

Seville: The rebel leader, Llanos, announced here on the radio today that the long-besieged city of Oviedo was occupied by the rebel army yesterday. The original besieged rebel army had 2,500 people. When the reinforcements entered the Oviedo church yesterday, only 300 people were found to be alive. It is claimed that more than 5,000 government troops died in the recent war in Oviedo. (National Telegram, 18th)

It is Rumored That the Spanish Government Plans to: Request the League of Nations to: Convene a Special Meeting of the Council: Invoke Article 11 of the Covenant

(Geneva) It is rumored that the Spanish government is now planning to invoke Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant and request that the League of Nations Council convene a special meeting to discuss the issue of the non-intervention agreement in the domestic turmoil being violated, especially when the Soviet government withdraws from the Non-Intervention Enforcement Committee. This request should be made. However, the League of Nations Secretary has not received any information. (Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant states that any situation that affects international relations and is sufficient to disrupt international peace or endanger the good understanding on which international peace depends, any member state of the League of Nations may request the Secretary-General to convene a meeting of the Council.) (Havas, 19th) According to the Asahi Shimbun, Minister of the Army Terauchi and Minister of the Navy Nagano have been strongly urging the government to implement administrative reforms. It has now been decided to ease this pressure and cooperate with Prime Minister Hirota in order to carry out gradual adjustments. The Prime Minister is willing to postpone this move until after the Diet session to avoid causing a cabinet crisis. This has also been accepted in principle by the Ministers of the Army and Navy. It is heard that the cabinet will now concentrate on preparing a new budget. (Reuters, 19th)

(Tokyo) The issue of electricity control, which will be handled by the government departments, is of great importance. After the three-minister meeting on the 18th, the original draft of the Ministry of Communications, which is based on private ownership and national operation, will be the main body. It has been decided to refer to the opposition and add several revised terms to approve it. In the afternoon of the 19th, Minister of Communications Riemumoto was added, and a four-minister meeting was held. After deliberations by the four related cabinet members, the government is now implementing one of its important national policies, electricity control, and the pending electricity issue has also been resolved in the government departments. Therefore, the government will focus all its efforts on compiling the budget for the coming year. The tax system reform related to it is being carefully studied by the Ministry of Finance. On the one hand, various provinces are now eager to review the budget and hold a budget cabinet meeting in mid-November. When compiling the budget, how to adjust the huge national defense budget and the budget required for the concretization of various national policies advocated by the government, and what is the issue of the limit of public debt issuance, are the most important issues in the budget compilation period. Therefore, Prime Minister Hirota, Minister of Finance Baba, Minister of the Army Terauchi, and Minister of the Navy Nagano will engage in frequent negotiations in the future. (Domei, 19th)

International Labor Maritime Conference: Passes Resolution: Advocates Improving the Residence of Seafarers

(Geneva) The Maritime Conference unanimously passed a resolution advocating that the residence of seafarers in anchoring ports should be improved. The measures include the construction of housing, the establishment of medical institutions, the formulation of health regulations, and the remittance of wages to their families. The Maritime Conference then passed a draft convention with 58 votes to 8 votes, advocating that those who serve as shipowners and officers of merchant ships should have a minimum level of competence. The British representative expressed opposition to this. (Havas, 19th)

Round-the-World Travel Race: Completing the Entire Journey in Three Weeks; Aikins First to Arrive in America

San Francisco - Mr. Aikins of the New York World Telegram recently competed with Mr. Merrillan of the New York Times and Ms. Kilgallen of International News Service in a race around the world by air and sea. Mr. Aikins arrived here today from Manila aboard the "China Clipper" airplane, making him the first of the three contestants to reach America. The other two will begin their return trip from Manila on Tuesday. This competition only allows the use of commercial airplanes, trains, and ships. The three departed simultaneously from Lakehurst, New Jersey, aboard the German airship "Hindenburg" on September 30th. After arriving in Frankfurt, they went their separate ways. Mr. Aikins was consistently in the lead. After arriving in Manila, he was delayed for several days due to bad weather. He then embarked on the "China Clipper" on October 16th. Mr. Aikins hopes to complete the entire journey within twenty days and return to Lakehurst. (Reuters telegram, 19th)

Hurricane Strikes Japan, Turns Toward Southeast Waters, Mainland Honshu May Be Spared Disaster

(Tokyo) A hurricane with a wind speed of 36.5 meters per second, which struck the Okinawa Islands and was expected to move towards Honshu, has since changed direction and turned northeast-east. At 6:00 AM on the 19th, it was moving at a speed of 25 kilometers per hour between southeast of Okinawa Island and South Daito Island. It will pass through the southern waters on the night of the 20th, so the disaster of the typhoon is thought to be unlikely to occur. (Domei News Agency telegram, 19th)

Earthquake Disaster in Venice

Venice - A strong earthquake occurred in the Venice region of Italy today. At least twenty people have been killed and one hundred and twenty injured. Two hundred houses have been cracked by the earthquake. The road from Victoria to Belluna has been cut off due to the road cracking. However, the biggest damage in the city of Venice is only the collapse of chimneys. Most of the victims were still asleep. Several people were injured when the bell tower of the Codiñeno Church collapsed. The Conelian Old Castle collapsed, killing fifteen people. A government bulletin stated that the public is quite calm. Relief workers have rushed to the Sassier district. The clocks in Venice all stopped at 4:12 AM. Most residents fled their homes to await the dawn. The second tremor at 2:00 AM caused the most alarm in Belluna, where many houses were cracked, but there were no casualties. (National News Agency telegram, 19th)

Certain Party Implements Poisoning of Chahar North, Heavy Opium Taxes, Farmers' Subtle Groans, Large Expansion of a Certain Party's Airport in Zhangbei

Zhangbei Communication: Since the six counties of Duolun, Guyuan, Baochang, Kangbao, Shangyi, and Shangdu in Chahar North were forcibly occupied by puppet troops last year, a special situation has been created, and a poisoning policy has been implemented to kill the people of Chahar North. The general jackals of a certain party, catering to the wishes of a certain party, ordered farmers to plant opium as a source of income for the puppet troops. At the beginning of opium planting, a five yuan opium tax was paid per acre. This income alone was considerable. After the farmers planted, additional taxes were repeatedly added, totaling no less than one yuan per acre. When the opium seedlings grew and were about to be harvested, the puppet government again issued a notice to the planting households in each county, requiring each acre of land to pay 30 taels of official opium, with an official price of 6 jiao per tael. Most of this official opium is used to supply a certain party for the manufacture of drugs. This year's opium in various counties in Chahar North, due to weather conditions, has not grown well, and the harvest is difficult to expect. The most miserable are the general poor farmers. The amount of land they own is already small. In order to seek immediate benefits, they have all abandoned farming and changed to opium. The food for the winter and spring seasons depends entirely on opium. Now encountering this situation, they all frown, groan, and complain bitterly. If the amount harvested per acre is not enough to pay the 30 taels to the government, the puppet government will purchase it at the official price of 6 jiao per tael, and then the puppet government will sell it at one yuan per tael. The taxes are extremely harsh, and the exploitation is heavy. The general farmers are almost left with nothing.

Looking at Zhangbei County, outside the East Gate, there is an airport built by a certain party, which is the largest of a certain party's airports in Chahar North. The original area has reached six hectares. At the beginning of this month, a certain party resumed expansion, and it has now reached about ten hectares. It still seems insufficient and is still under active construction. Li Shouxin himself is currently in Zhangbei, working very hard every day. He has also transferred 500 elite troops from various puppet units under his command and reorganized them into a special task force for active training. Since Li invaded Chahar North last year, although his troops have nominally expanded to five divisions, in reality there are only more than 2,600 people. Most of the troops are cavalry. However, Li seems to take the training of his subordinates extremely seriously. He must take time every day to supervise the training ground. His troop camps are all inside and outside Zhangbei County. Other bandit troops have now all left. There is only Wang Ying's military station in the city. The station is currently purchasing a large amount of food and transporting it to Shangdu for military rations. In the past two months, there have often been six aircraft stationed at the airport outside the East Gate, flying to Suidong from time to time for reconnaissance. (16th)

Road Construction and Bandit Suppression in Northeastern Fujian, Pacification Headquarters Has Been Moved to Jian'ou

Fuzhou Communication: Jiang Dingwen, the Director of Pacification stationed in Fujian, has moved the Pacification Headquarters from Zhangzhou to Jian'ou in order to supervise the construction of the northeastern Fujian highway and suppress scattered bandits. The headquarters started to move on the 14th of this month in three batches. The first batch, led by Adjutant He Guozhen and six others, arrived in the province by car from Zhangzhou on the 16th, along with the guards, and will go to Jian'ou on the 18th to arrange the new Pacification Headquarters. The second batch, led by Adjutant Director Feng Chizhong and others, will transport equipment to the province around the 20th and then to Jian'ou. The third batch, led by Chief of Staff Li Jianai and others, will bring files to the province and then to Jian'ou before the 25th. As for Jiang Dingwen, he arrived in Xiamen from Zhangzhou on the 15th and plans to visit Chairman Chiang in Hangzhou first, and then go to the northeastern Fujian Pacification Headquarters in Minbei from Zhejiang. After the move to Jian'ou, it is heard that Li Yangjing, the Commander of Qingxiang in the Fujian-Zhejiang-Jiangxi border area, will set up his headquarters in Zhangzhou.

The northeastern Fujian highway project, from Jiangshan on the Zhejiang border through Pucheng in Fujian Province to Jian'ou, is now open to traffic. The section from Jian'ou through Shaowu to Guangze on the Jiangxi border is currently under construction and will be completed in ten days. The section from Ningde through Fuding to Taishun on the Zhejiang border is now ordered by the Military Affairs Commission to use military labor to open up construction simultaneously in both provinces, and to complete it in a short period of time. The Construction Department will send engineers to guide the work in the coming days.

As for the bandit situation, the remnants of bandits in northern Fujian were previously under tight search and suppression by the army, and their supply routes were cut off. Their food was exhausted, and the situation was extremely difficult. Recently, taking advantage of the movement of the army, they harassed the area again, often falsely using the name of Huang Ligui to confuse the public and exaggerate their power. They also plan to rob farmers of their newly harvested autumn grain. Jianyang, Jianguo, Shaowu, Jiangle, and Shunchang counties have suffered the most. In recent days, the people of various counties in northern Fujian have asked the Provincial Government and Pacification Headquarters to quickly dispatch troops to suppress the bandits in order to prevent the bandits from growing stronger. In eastern Fujian, since the stationed troops were transferred to other places a month ago, the bandit forces have also spread again. Recently, the remnants of Liu Ying's troops have fled from the Jiangxi border into Fuding, and their strength has been restored. The entire county, except for the county seat, has almost no place without traces of bandits. The so-called pseudo-Su troops are even more ruthless in killing dissidents. The people are extremely panicked and flee into the city in groups. The provincial government has been informed and has ordered the Huang Su troops of the 2nd Security Regiment stationed in Gutian to rush to suppress them. (October 17th)

Guangdong's Industry and Commerce Are Declining Daily; Government and Banks Conduct Loan Relief; Business Community Asks for Low-Interest Loans to Revive Finance

Guangzhou Communication: In recent years, due to the decline of industry and commerce in Guangdong Province, the sharp decline in exports, and the annual trade deficit, the social finance has been gradually exhausted. Today, the situation is becoming increasingly strained. Most of the originally large stores have closed down, and the few remaining small-capital factories are in a precarious situation. Those who care about the national economy cannot help but shudder. According to a recent survey, in the province's industries, except for one or two state-run factories that are slightly profitable due to controlled operations, in Guangzhou's private factories, there are only two with capital of more than 200,000 yuan, three with more than 50,000 yuan, and 24 with more than 10,000 yuan. The state of decline is evident. The authorities have the intention of providing relief. In addition to the tobacco leaf loan previously organized by the Department of Finance, borrowing 2 million yuan from the Shanghai Bank to develop the native tobacco leaf in Nanxiong, they have recently negotiated with the Shanghai banking community to borrow 10 million yuan, with monthly interest between six and eight percent. The government will provide considerable collateral. The loan is intended to develop the silk and cotton industries, etc. Regarding the loan to develop sericulture and weaving in Shunde, it is heard that the Provincial Bank and the Shanghai Jiaotong Bank will jointly handle it. The Provincial Bank previously sent staff to Shunde and the surrounding areas for investigation, which has now been completed. Once the Jiaotong Bank sends staff south to negotiate a solution, the loan plan can be signed with local silk factories. The Department of Construction has recently formulated plans to develop private water conservancy, chemical industry, mining, fisheries, dyeing and silk industry, and stationery manufacturing industry, etc., welcoming investment from overseas Chinese in Nanyang and Hong Kong merchants. Looking at the above matters, some are in the planning stage, and some have been realized. It may not be a good hope for the future of Guangdong's industries. However, on the merchants' side, there are also people who want to independently run industries and expand businesses, but they cannot do anything without resources due to years of losses. Therefore, in recent days, most merchants have requested the Municipal Industry Federation to forward a letter to the government, asking the provincial and municipal banks to provide large loans to maintain the existing commerce and seek development. The Industry Federation received the letter and has presented it to the Department of Finance yesterday, asking the municipal bank to handle it. The letter stated, "Since our city was attacked by the world economic depression, the financial situation has become increasingly exhausted, and industry and commerce have been declining daily. The suffering of merchants and people is difficult to describe. In the blink of an eye, the end of the year is approaching, and the demand for funds is extremely urgent. If we do not provide timely relief, then the turnover will definitely feel inflexible, collapse one after another, and fall into a state of no return. The people are waiting to be rescued from their predicament, and the government's tax revenue will also be lost in conjunction. (Excerpt) The current phenomenon of decline cannot be rescued without the government banks providing large amounts of credit to revive the withered fish. Therefore, last month, we presented a request to order the provincial and municipal banks to allocate 20 million yuan in legal currency, allowing the people to mortgage their industries to obtain funds for turnover. Later, the Provincial Bank released a small number of loans, which can temporarily help at the moment, but it is not enough to maintain the overall situation. Now, we see that the times are difficult and funds are scarce, and all industries are on the verge of extinction, urgently waiting for fresh troops to save them from danger. If the request is realized in the short term, the citizens' real estate can be transformed into circulating gold, not only will the financial situation be active, but all industries will be revived, and the industry will also rise accordingly. Overseas Chinese will inevitably hear the news and be inspired to bring back their capital stored in foreign banks to invest in real estate. The municipality will prosper accordingly, and tax revenue will also increase immeasurably. In this transition, both the public and private sectors will receive great benefits (Excerpt). We hereby submit a document to your department, asking you to approve it and order the provincial and municipal banks to raise 20 million yuan, carefully formulate regulations for industrial mortgages, stipulate a weekly interest rate of five to six percent, with a term of half a year. After the expiration, permission will still be granted to clear the interest and renew the single, release credit on a regular basis, and announce it widely to help the financial situation." (October 17th)

If this work is completed, Japanese cotton can be sold all over the world.

Wuxi: Yarn and Cloth Cannot Meet Demand

There are four or five weaving factories in the county, including Shenxin, Guangfeng, Guangqin, and Lixin. The internal facilities are very complete and the products are of high quality and are popular with people from all over the country. In the past half month, the market price of cotton yarn in the city has soared, which is a rare phenomenon in recent years. The Shen standard has risen to nearly 20 yuan per piece. The market price in the city has also risen accordingly, with each brand rising by 8 or 9 yuan per piece. People in the market are still unanimously bullish. On the 18th, the market price of each brand of cotton yarn rose again by several jiao to one yuan. According to people in the cotton yarn industry, the reason for the rise in the yarn market is that cotton sales have been smooth recently. Cotton weaving manufacturers have purchased large quantities of cotton yarn as much as possible, and the yarn appearing in the factory cannot meet the demand, resulting in soaring market prices. As for the reason for the smooth sales of cotton cloth, it is that the autumn harvest this year is abundant, and the rural economy is gradually recovering. At this cool autumn season, farmers are adding new clothes, and because Zhuang Ding training is being held everywhere this year, uniforms must be worn uniformly, so cotton cloth has a special sales route. In the future, the market price still has a tendency to continue to rise.

Silk Cocoon Market Price is Firm

Since the spring cocoons entered the market, the silk factories in the city have started their operations one after another. Until recently, the number of silk factories that have started their operations in the city and countryside has reached 36, with about 10,000 silk machines. All of them are profitable. Most of the dried cocoons stored in various factories can be worked until the end of the year. As for the market price of Chinese silk, since August, the European and American silk markets have been rising again. The weaving factories in New York and other places are gradually importing as autumn sales have arrived and the inventory of raw silk is not abundant. At present, the highest white factory of Chinese silk can be sold at more than 730 yuan per load, 13 or 15 standard high-white classics can be sold at 690 yuan per group, and 20 or 12 standard ordinary silk can also be sold at 650 yuan. Compared with the previous low market price, it has risen by 30 or 40 yuan. As for the market price of dried cocoons, it is currently rising with it, at 150 yuan per load. Observing the situation, there is still a tendency to continue to rise. Chen Qixiang and Ni Lisheng, silk cocoon merchants in Dongting Town, Second District, pooled more than 5,000 yuan to create a small silk factory in Xintang Bridge in view of the better silk market. They are preparing to install more than 100 silk machines. They are currently renovating the houses and working day and night. They must start work at the beginning of the month. The future of silk cocoons is gradually becoming optimistic.

Changzhou Seventh District Murder Case

Pan Yinchuan, from Dongjietou, Caoxi Township, Seventh District of Wu County, has a son named Ronghai, aged twenty-seven. Recently, Xu Laoer from Dongtai acted as a matchmaker, and he married the daughter of Jiang Zhicheng from Houyu. The wedding was originally scheduled for the fifteenth of this month, but due to travel fatigue on that day, it was changed to the sixteenth for ancestral rites. During the ceremony, Zhang Canru and Wang Qiudao suddenly demanded repayment of debts from Xu Laoer, arguing for a long time outside the Pan family's gate. This led to a fight, and Xu, being outnumbered, was struck in a vital area and collapsed to the ground, dying shortly after. The groom, Ronghai, realizing he had caused trouble, ran to inform the Jia head, who reported it to the local court. On the seventeenth, the court sent officials to the village for an autopsy and took Pan Ronghai into the city for interrogation. One account says that Pan Ronghai borrowed money from the matchmaker Xu Laoer when he got engaged, and Xu demanded repayment on the sixteenth. Ronghai then incited the guests to beat Xu Laoer to death, making Ronghai the real culprit, who was arrested for investigation. The local prosecutor's office opened a court hearing on the eighteenth and questioned Pan Ronghai, who vehemently denied inciting the murder. The court then ordered his detention, pending the arrest and investigation of other perpetrators.

Zhenjiang Canal Water Storage for Navigation

Xu Dingkang, director of the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau, stated that since autumn, the canal's water level has been gradually decreasing. Recently, it has dropped by more than five inches. The Qingjiang Zheng Gate records show that the canal's water level is only one zhang and eight chi and three cun, a decrease of one zhang compared to the high-water season. Due to the drop in water level, areas around Mapengwan and Jieshou are gradually becoming dry, and there is a risk of squeezing the river. Director Xu decided to close all the gate openings along the canal, as well as the Phoenix and Dongluo gates, to store water for navigation. Additionally, planting season has passed in the counties south of the canal, so there is no need to drain water. He has now telegraphed Qi Shou'an, director of the Jiangshi section of the works department, as well as Jiangdu, Gaobao, and Huaian counties, ordering them to immediately close all gate openings and dams along the canal to store water for navigation. After closing the gates, all shipping can proceed without obstruction, and the Jizhen ferry can also operate smoothly.

Xiaoshan Shengjiawu Major Fire

At 2:15 PM on the fifteenth, a fire broke out in the home of Sheng Alian, a resident of Shengjiawu in eastern Xiaoshan, due to carelessly leaving a fire in the firewood while making tea. As the weather was dry and there had been no rain, everything was susceptible to fire, and it quickly spread to the neighboring firewood shed. In an instant, the flames soared into the sky and then spread to the wealthy Sheng Pinshan's house. The smoke filled the air, and the home of the gentry Sheng Lianxin was also in danger. The two Yilong rescue teams from Shuangfengtang had already arrived after hearing the alarm. They worked hard to protect and extinguish the fire at Sheng Lianxin's large residence, but the corner of the east wing had already been reduced to ashes. Eight houses were damaged, with forty-five rooms burned. Sheng Pinshan suffered the greatest losses, with over three thousand liang of silkworm silk from the past four to five years, stored and unsold, and other belongings, all unable to be moved out and burned. Pinshan is Sheng Lianxin's uncle and is quite wealthy. After inspecting the eight houses, the losses are estimated to be over 20,000 gold. The fire was extinguished from 2:15 PM to 4:40 PM.

Cixi Rice Mill Bankrupt and Closed

Hengji Rice Mill in Qiushe Town, eastern Cixi, was established by the current town mayor, Mai Yuanji, with his own investment. It has been open for over ten years, and its business was doing well. Since the decline of the rural economy, the mill has been superficially strong but internally weak, struggling to maintain operations. Due to excessive losses, it was finally announced to close down the other day. It is estimated that over 20,000 yuan is owed to various depositors, who are now requesting repayment. Mediation for repayment is underway.

Recent Situation in Guangdong and Guangxi (6)

— Our Reporter Xiao'an

Guangzhou's Municipal Administration (Part 1)

Guangzhou established its municipal government in the seventh year of the Republic, initially named the Municipal Office. In the tenth year of the Republic, the Municipal Hall was established. In the seventeenth year, the Municipal Hall was renamed the Special Municipal Government. In the eighteenth year, the special municipal system was abolished and named the Guangzhou Municipal Government. It remains as such to this day. The current location is behind Central Park and operates as a joint office, but only the Finance, Land, Health, and Public Works Bureaus are attached. The Social, Public Utilities, and Education Bureaus, as well as the Water Management Office, Electricity Management Office, and Telephone Committee, are not located there. During the tenures of former mayors Cheng Tiangu and Liu Jiwen, although there was much talk of municipal construction, the dirtiness of the city and the disorderliness of the order still left a residual influence that has not been entirely eradicated. Furthermore, the citizens have had a negative impression of things such as the licensing of citizen's construction and the acceptance of students at city schools. Therefore, although Guangzhou has had a new municipal administration for more than ten years, it has not truly satisfied the citizens.

Since the current mayor, Zeng Yangfu, took office on August 10th of this year, it has been heard that he has been striving to reduce municipal expenses. Therefore, he abolished the Public Utilities and Education Bureaus and the new power plant. Public utilities affairs have been merged into the Public Works Bureau, education affairs have been merged into the Social Bureau, and new power plant affairs have been merged into the Electricity Management Office. At the same time, he is determined to move forward with all facilities, likely learning from the mistakes of previous mayors and hoping to remedy and innovate. The reporter visited Mayor Zeng at the Municipal Government. Mayor Zeng informed me in great detail about the recent central work of the various bureaus of the Municipal Government. Here is a brief description to give a glimpse:

Matters concerning the Social Bureau: (1) Conducting a population survey. Guangzhou City conducted a population survey in October of the twenty-first year of the Republic. It has been four years since then, and there have been changes. The Social Bureau plans to conduct a new survey in conjunction with the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau to obtain clear data. (2) Reorganizing social organizations. Many of Guangzhou's social organizations have not complied with the central regulations in terms of organization and dynamics over the past seven years. The Social Bureau plans to create a form to be filled out and send personnel for strict inspection, guiding them back on the right track and strengthening their organization. (3) Inspecting factories. The Social Bureau believes that the rise and fall of labor affairs depend on whether the factory law can be effectively implemented. Assessing its performance requires inspection to determine its quality. The bureau plans to create a form to be filled out by each factory and order them to organize welfare and labor affairs. (4) Promoting the national language. The Social Bureau plans to divide all city schools in the city into fifteen districts, with two national language study classes in each district. All teachers and staff of the city schools will join the study, with a five-month duration. (5) Registering teachers. The qualifications of teachers in Guangzhou schools are quite uneven, and many are not suitable for the subjects they teach. Moreover, they are all recommended and appointed by the principals. The Social Bureau plans to conduct a registration of teachers in municipal primary schools, limiting qualifications to normal school graduates. Military training will be provided during the winter vacation, and a committee will be set up to assist in the process. (6) Eliminating illiteracy. According to the city's population survey report in the twenty-first year of the Republic, 396,000 people were illiterate. The Social Bureau is now planning to launch a mass literacy campaign, establishing 1,000 literacy schools attached to various schools in the city, with a three-month duration. It is estimated that within two years, illiteracy in the city can be completely eliminated. (7) Expanding relief efforts. There are many poor people in Guangzhou City, and the relief homes only accommodate 5,000 people, making expansion necessary. Institutions such as orphanages, women's vocational training centers, and agricultural and forestry farms should also be increased. Nursing homes, infant daycare centers, and workers' residences also need to be built. The Social Bureau is planning and implementing all of these. (8) Rectifying charitable organizations. Abuses often occur in charitable organizations in the city. Therefore, the Social Bureau has specifically drafted measures to send personnel for detailed investigation and strict assessment for cleaning and rectification. (9) Job placement. Recently, various industries have declined, and unemployment has increased. Therefore, the Social Bureau plans to organize various labor job registrations, worker unemployment registrations, specialized talent unemployment registrations, and investigations of various public utilities, mechanical industries, and handicrafts, and employer investigations to implement job placement. (10) Editing and reviewing plays. The Social Bureau believes that various plays and scripts for actresses contain obscene and superstitious words. Therefore, it plans to hire people with playwriting knowledge to form a playwriting committee with the Guangzhou City Drama, Film, and Song Review Committee to provide guidance and remedy, guiding them towards goodness. (11) Increasing loans. The Social Bureau has provided small vendor loans with a fund of 2,000 yuan and household industry loans with a fund of 10,000 yuan, which citizens have found convenient. Now, the Social Bureau plans to raise more funds to increase circulation, increasing the small vendor loan fund to 5,000 yuan and the household industry loan fund to 30,000 yuan.

Matters concerning the Health Bureau: (1) Universal immunization, (2) Prevention of infectious diseases, (3) Treatment of infectious diseases, (4) Establishing a smoking cessation hospital, (5) Reorganizing and expanding municipal hospitals, (6) Medical and pharmaceutical management, (7) Opening public health and other personnel training classes, (8) Popularizing health knowledge.

Matters concerning the Land Bureau: (1) Continuing forced land registration, (2) Completing the registration book, (3) Estimating land prices, (4) Temporary land tax, (5) Applying for surveying, (6) Boundary re-measurement, (7) Compiling cadastral maps, (8) Compiling cadastral registers.

Page 9

Local News

Our Nation's Literary Giant, Lu Xun, Passed Away Yesterday Morning; The Encoffining Ceremony Will Be Held Tomorrow Afternoon at the International Funeral Home; Burial at the International Cemetery on the 22nd

Lu Xun, our nation's literary giant, suffered from severe lung disease and was once on the verge of death this summer. After treatment in Shanghai, he gradually recovered. On the 17th, due to excessive walking and talking, his condition suddenly deteriorated, and he suffered from severe shortness of breath and could not sleep. Despite emergency medical treatment, he passed away at approximately 5 AM yesterday morning. His body was moved to the International Funeral Home, and the encoffining ceremony is scheduled for tomorrow afternoon, with burial at the International Cemetery on the 22nd. The details of his passing are reported below:

Passed Away Yesterday Morning

Mr. Lu Xun passed away at 5:25 AM yesterday morning at his residence at No. 9 Continental New Village, Shigaota Road. After the news spread, his relatives and friends, including Madam Song Qingling, Hu Feng, Uchiyama Kanzo, Hu Yuzhi, and others, went to offer their condolences. Woodcarver Li Qun also rushed to carve his posthumous portrait. His body was taken by a hearse sent by the International Funeral Home at 3 PM and was cosmetically prepared and encoffined. It was placed in the auditorium on the second floor. Those who came to pay their respects upon hearing the news included Shen Junru, Li Gongpu, Zou Taofen, Yao Ke, Ba Jin, Zhang Tianyi, Shen Zijiu, Ikeda Sachiko, Hasegawa Saburo, Ouyang Shan, and others, who paid their respects to the deceased and comforted his family.

Obituary and Funeral Arrangements

Lu Xun's body, after being moved to the International Funeral Home, will be open for condolences from all circles today and tomorrow. Burial will be at the Hongqiao International Cemetery on the 22nd. A funeral committee has been formed by Cai Yuanpei, Ma Xiangbo, Song Qingling, Uchiyama Kanzo, Smedley, Shen Junru, Mao Dun, Xiao Can, and others to handle all arrangements. An obituary was issued yesterday stating: "Mr. Lu Xun (Zhou Shuren) passed away from illness at his Shanghai residence at 5:25 AM on October 19, 1936, at the age of 56. His body will be moved to the International Funeral Home today. From 10 AM to 5 PM on the 20th, the public is invited to pay their respects. In accordance with Mr. Lu Xun's wishes, 'No one should receive a single penny for the funeral.' Except for sacrificial offerings, condolences, and wreaths, all monetary gifts are declined. This obituary is hereby issued."

Last Writings

During his life, he and his wife, Madam Xu Guangping, were deeply in love. Therefore, when he was ill, his wife personally prepared his medicine and cared for him diligently, almost without rest. Now that he has passed away, her grief is extreme. He leaves behind a son, only seven years old, named Haiying, who is studying at Continental Primary School and also attended to his father's side. According to Madam Xu, Mr. Lu Xun's condition worsened on the 17th, and he could not sleep. However, his mind was clear. Only his shortness of breath was severe. He did not leave any last words. He recently had an essay, "Death," published in the second issue of Zhongliu magazine, in which he drafted a will. At the time, it was only a literary composition, but it has now become a prophecy. In the future, it will be followed as he had written in his will.

Content of the Will

The seven articles of the will are transcribed below: (1) No one should receive a single penny for the funeral, but old friends are exempt from this rule. (2) Arrange the encoffining and burial quickly and be done with it. (3) Do not do anything related to commemoration. (4) Forget me and take care of your own life. If not, then you are truly a confused insect. (5) If the child grows up and has no talent, find some small things to live on, but do not become an empty-headed literary or art critic. (6) Do not take things that others allow you to have too seriously. (7) Do not approach those who harm others' teeth and eyes but oppose revenge and advocate tolerance.

Medical Treatment

According to Mr. Lu Xun's close friend, Uchiyama Kanzo, the course of his illness was as follows: He suffered from pulmonary tuberculosis and was once on the verge of death this summer, treated by Dr. Suto. He had gradually recovered, and the doctor ordered him to move to Nagasaki Unsen for treatment, but it did not happen. Therefore, he rested in Shanghai. He still wrote this month. At 3 PM on the 17th, he took a walk in Hongkou Park. On the way back, he chatted with three or five friends at Uchiyama Bookstore for half an hour. At that time, the north wind was strong, so he quickly returned to rest. However, due to overwork, he suddenly developed a fever and severe shortness of breath. He could not sleep well at night. The next day, Dr. Suto was called for treatment. Because the situation was very dangerous, Dr. Song Bing from Fumin Hospital and Dr. Ishii from Ishii Hospital were consulted in the afternoon.

Final Moments

At that time, fearing a sudden change, a nurse, Tajima, was assigned to take care of him. Every 30 minutes, oxygen was inhaled to help his breathing, and cardiotonic injections were given. If there were no changes within two days, he could overcome the crisis. However, at approximately 5 AM yesterday morning, his breathing became more rapid. Three injections were ineffective. At 5:25 AM, he passed away from cardiac arrest. Only his wife, Madam Xu, his younger brother, Jianren, and the nurse were present.

Zhou's Life

Lu Xun, originally named Zhou Shuren, was from Shaoxing, Zhejiang. His family was poor in his youth. At the age of eighteen, he entered the Nanjing Naval Academy as a scholarship student. Later, he went to Japan to study at medical school. Before the Xinhai Revolution, he joined the Restoration Society and engaged in the national revolutionary movement. He also began to promote new literature. Three years before the Republic of China, he returned to China and successively served as a teacher at Shaoxing Normal School, a professor at Peking University, Xiamen University, and Guangzhou Zhongshan University. During the May Fourth Movement, he began to publish "Diary of a Madman" in New Youth magazine under the pen name Lu Xun, becoming a realist writer. In addition to novels, his sharp essays were widely circulated. His major works include the novels "Call to Arms" and "Wandering," and the essays "Hot Wind," "Huagai Collection," and "E'er Collection." He translated no less than dozens of works, including "A Youth's Dream," "Peach-Colored Clouds," "Fairy Tales," and "Art Theory." He passed away at the age of 56. His mother is still alive. His wife is Madam Xu Guangping, and his son, Haiying, is only seven years old. His elder brother, Zuoren, is a professor at Peking University, and his younger brother, Jianren, is an editor at the Commercial Press.

Japanese Friends Mourn

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo: After the news of the death of Chinese literary giant Lu Xun reached here, Japanese writers such as Aono Suekichi, Hayashi Fusao, Akita Ujaku, Fujimori Seikichi, Sato Haruo, Ishihama Tomoyuki, and Oka Kunio all expressed their grief. They all believed that Lu Xun's literary cultivation was profound and his social thought was outstanding. He was a star among the writers of Eastern countries. His sudden death is a huge loss to the world's literary and cultural scene. Akita Ujaku and others have launched a fundraising campaign to cast a bronze statue of this Eastern literary giant to commemorate him.

Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions Asks the Municipal Government to Negotiate with the Japanese Army on Cross-Border Patrols

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation presented a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating, "Regarding the petition, since the start of Sino-Japanese diplomatic negotiations, the people of the country have been looking forward to candid discussions and the adjustment of national relations to lay the foundation for peace in East Asia. However, the Japanese army stationed in Shanghai has been conducting cross-border patrols and setting up posts everywhere to interrogate pedestrians, causing public anxiety and unrest. This matter has been negotiated with the government before, but it has not been stopped. We believe that the Shanghai market has been extremely depressed since the January 28th Incident, and this impact makes the future unbearable. We respectfully request that the government continue negotiations to stop the Japanese army's cross-border patrols to reassure residents and maintain the market. We sincerely pray for this."

Vigorous Gauze Trade and Soaring Prices; China Economic News Briefly Suspended Publication; Evening Session Extended to 9 PM

Shen Shi News Agency reports that the Shanghai Chinese Gauze Exchange is seeing increasingly strong sales of gauze, resulting in supply falling short of demand. Demand from various groups was very high yesterday, with spot gauze prices soaring by 17 or 18 yuan and the money price jumping by 40 yuan. Forward prices also rose sharply. Yesterday morning, there was a lot of trading in the opening session. The market closed at 2:30 PM. The current month rose sharply by four yuan, and the second session jumped another four yuan before trading was suspended. November, December, January, February, and March also closed up eight to five yuan. The evening session did not open until 4:30 PM, but the public was still bullish, leading to strong buying interest and higher gauze prices. The session did not close until about 9:00 PM. As a result, each month rose by more than eight yuan, and the buying interest remained strong.

Mr. Zhang Hui Talks About Overseas Chinese Affairs in Cuba

More Than 20,000 Overseas Chinese Live Peacefully; A New Chinese School Has Been Established

Mr. Zhang Hui, the Chinese Minister to Cuba, who has returned to China on leave, arrived in Shanghai on the President Coolidge on the 18th. He decided to go to Beijing last night to report to Foreign Minister Zhang. Then he will quickly return to his hometown in Guangdong Province to visit his relatives. Yesterday morning, the reporter specially visited Mr. Zhang at his residence. The following is a record of Mr. Zhang's talk about the situation of overseas Chinese affairs in Cuba:

Reporting Duties in Beijing

Mr. Zhang has been serving as the envoy to Cuba for more than a year. This time, he took leave to return to China on September 25, first taking a plane from Havana to Los Angeles in the United States. Then he took the President Coolidge of the Dollar Steamship Lines eastward to return home. According to Mr. Zhang's conversation with the reporter, he decided to take three months of leave. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, he must also return to his hometown in Zhongshan County, Guangdong Province, to visit his relatives. Because his father has been suffering from madness, and the illness has become quite severe, he is anxious to take leave to return home. He decided to take the 11 o'clock express train to Beijing last night to pay respects to Foreign Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to report everything. Whether he will go to Hangzhou to see President Chiang Kai-shek will be decided after arriving in Beijing. After reporting to the government, he will still come to Shanghai to take a ship back to Guangdong Province to visit his relatives.

The Situation of Overseas Chinese

Mr. Zhang continued to talk about the situation of overseas Chinese in Cuba. According to statistics, there are about 30,000 overseas Chinese living in Cuba, most of whom are from Guangdong, Fujian, and Zhejiang provinces. They are engaged in small businesses such as groceries and laundry, as well as working for a living. In recent years, due to the impact of the global economic downturn, the restrictions imposed by the local government, and the competition from local workers, it has become somewhat difficult to make a living, resulting in unemployed overseas Chinese. Fortunately, overseas Chinese there have organizations similar to hometown associations, which help each other. Accommodation is not a problem, so there are no wandering and destitute overseas Chinese.

Establishing Education

Although the number of overseas Chinese there reaches more than 30,000, there has never been a school established by overseas Chinese, so that the overseas Chinese growing up in Cuba are completely ignorant of the Chinese language. When I first took office, in view of the concern that overseas Chinese children would be unable to attend school, I summoned powerful overseas Chinese there to establish a school. After seven or eight months of preparatory work, a "Chinese School" has now been established in Havana, the capital of Cuba, to accommodate as many overseas Chinese children as possible. The school opened on October 1 last year. In addition to the donations from overseas Chinese, the government also provides considerable subsidies. After this initial education has achieved results, it will be gradually promoted so that overseas Chinese education will not decline.

Cuban Politics

Regarding the diplomatic relations between China and Cuba, they have always been cordial. The governments and people of both countries treat each other with an extremely friendly attitude. Cuba is a country in South America, and all its political facilities mostly imitate the United States. In recent years, the political situation has been very stable. The main language is Spanish, and the main products are sugar and tobacco, which are sold to various South American countries. The total population of the country is more than 4 million, and there are more than 600,000 foreigners, with about 1,000 foreigners entering the country every day, all engaged in planting for a living.
