The United States-China Bank Case: Three More Plaintiffs Added; Bao Ziwen and Chen Yizai Interrogated Separately; Both Released on Bail with Lawyers' Written Guarantees

Following the collapse of the United States-China Bank, numerous creditors have filed criminal charges of fraud and embezzlement with the First Special District Court against Gu Yubo and others responsible for the bank. Some creditors have even included Lin Kanghou, Shen Jingzhong, Qian Chengxu, Jiang Baili, and others who initiated the Dasin Bank (the predecessor to the United States-China Bank) as defendants, leading to multiple court hearings. Except for Jiang Baili, who has already gone abroad and had his lawsuit withdrawn by the plaintiffs, Gu Yubo and Liu Tongfu are wanted by the court, and Sun Wenkui has been placed under the responsibility of his

defense lawyer

Lin Yingqing, who secured his release on bail. The other defendants await further investigation. This newspaper has been reporting on these developments. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng continued the trial. The defendants who personally appeared were Bao Ziwen, Chen Yizai, Sun Wenkui, and Wang Zhonglin. Zhang Xusheng, Li Yichou, and Lin Kanghou were represented by lawyers Qian Zheng, Tang Huaiqun, Xu Jie, Wang Chuang'e, and others. Qian Chengxu and Wu Chunlei remained absent despite being summoned. Furthermore, the plaintiffs have added Chen Yimin, Zhang Yaojun, and Chen Peilun, bringing the total number of plaintiff households to twenty-four, alleging

embezzlement and fraud

amounting to over forty to fifty thousand yuan. In court, given the close relationship between defendants Bao and Chen, they were interrogated separately. Bao Ziwen was questioned first and stated that he was originally from Shaoxing and a salt merchant. Dasin Bank was planned the year before last with a capital of 500,000 yuan. He and Chen jointly subscribed for 50,000 yuan, which was handed over to Gu Yubo for collection, and he held Gu's receipt. Since the bank did not open, he did not receive formal stock certificates. He claimed to be unaware of the subsequent change to the United States-China Bank. The plaintiff's attorney, Wu Peng, then presented a photograph of the merger agreement between Dasin and the United States-China Bank and a photograph of Bao as a standing director of the United States-China Bank, as well as

United States-China Bank opening

telegrams of congratulations sent to the standing directors from other cities. After the court reviewed these documents, they were shown to Bao, but Bao still claimed to be unaware of the United States-China Bank's affairs. Judge Huang instructed him, "You are one of the founders of Dasin Bank and a standing director of the United States-China Bank. How can you claim to be unaware of the merger and the opening of the United States-China Bank? Moreover, after the merger, there was a board meeting, and your signature is on the record. You should explain the United States-China Bank's operations and the location of its account books. You cannot evade responsibility with mere excuses." However, Bao firmly denied serving as a standing director and said he

had no way to account

Bao's defense lawyer, Jiang Yiping, then presented the United States-China Bank's circular book, proving that Bao and Chen had never gone to the bank to handle affairs. He also presented a letter proving that Bao and Chen had not yet taken up their positions as directors. He then presented a photograph of the opening day of the United States-China Bank, stating that Bao was not in it, and further defended Bao and Chen, arguing that their 50,000 yuan had also been swindled away by Gu. Chen Yizai, when questioned, also denied being a shareholder or deputy manager of the United States-China Bank, claiming that the 15,000 yuan he had paid was for Dasin Bank shares. However, attorney Wu then presented a book of minutes from the United States-China Bank's western director meetings, stating that Chen and Bao's

duties

were clearly recorded in these minutes. Western directors such as Meng Lei and others were willing to appear in court as witnesses under subpoena. Therefore, there was no way to deny it with empty words. Subsequently, the court questioned Sun Wenkui, Wang Zhonglin, and the liquidators one by one, and ordered that the cases be adjourned to the afternoon of October 30 for further hearing. Bao Ziwen and Chen Yizai were ordered to each post an 8,000 yuan shop guarantee. Lawyer Jiang, upon hearing the order, repeatedly requested for Bao and Chen that the amount of the guarantee be reduced, otherwise they would not be able to afford it. Judge Huang then ordered lawyer Jiang to be responsible for bailing out the two defendants with a written guarantee pending trial.

After Ma Loufen Was Convicted of Adultery, His Wife Filed for Divorce; Mediation Failed Yesterday

Ma Loufen, a film actor from Suzhou, aged 27, married Bai Suzhen (aged 21) from Beiping. They lived with his parents at 16 Xing Shun Nan Li, Remi Road in the French Concession. They had a daughter named Die Nv, and their marital relationship was good. However, Ma led the Star Singing and Dancing Troupe to perform in Southeast Asia. During the trip, he had a relationship with Wei Dixian, a 19-year-old troupe member from Hangzhou, and upon returning to Shanghai, he took her as a concubine, renting a house at 266 La Du Road from August 1 to cohabit with her. He neglected his wife, Bai. On the night of the 2nd of this month, Ma's wife, Bai, reported to the French police that Ma was committing adultery with Wei, disrupting the family. The head of the police station dispatched detectives to arrest Ma and Wei and handed them over to the Special Second Court for public prosecution. After the trial, Ma Loufen and Wei Dixian were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment, suspended for three years. Now, Ma's wife, Bai, through her lawyer, Jia Lu, filed a petition with the Civil Division of the Special Court, requesting mediation to divorce her husband, Ma Loufen, and for the payment of alimony. Upon receiving the petition, the court, yesterday morning, presided over by Judge Song in the Civil Court No. 4, summoned both parties for mediation. The petitioner, Ma Bai, stated that since her husband had committed adultery and cohabited with Wei Dixian, he had not returned home and had neglected her. She had also been abused by her in-laws, leaving her no choice but to request mediation for divorce. The opposing party, Ma Loufen, stated that he opposed the divorce. His wife also knew about his marriage to Wei. They initially lived in the same house, but because they did not get along, he moved out to live separately. He had not abused his wife, and they had always been on good terms. He did not know why she had suddenly filed a complaint. After examining the arguments, the court, noting that both parties held firm to their positions, announced that mediation had failed and instructed the petitioner to file a formal lawsuit.

Elder Brother Seduces Sister-in-Law; Does Not Know What Shame Is; Neither Man Nor Woman Allowed Bail

Chen Caiyuan, from Yuyao, aged 69, has two sons. The elder, Chen Jinwen, aged 39, works at the Gold Exchange. The younger, Chen Jinrong, aged 22, used to run a coal shop and is now unemployed. Chen Yurong is married to Chen Ni, also aged 22. They used to live together in Huasheng Road, Zhabei, with only a board separating the brothers' rooms. However, Chen Jinrong had been unemployed for a long time and was short of money. He could not afford his wife's extravagance. Chen Jinwen, on the other hand, was lustful. Therefore, Jinwen coveted his young sister-in-law, while Ni envied her brother-in-law's wealth. Thus, an affair began. Chen Yurong eventually discovered it and began to monitor them. Chen Jinwen and Ni, after a heated discussion, first had Chen Jinwen move out, residing at 162 Kongjia Wood Bridge, Zhongxing Road. Then, on the 11th of last month, he instructed Ni to run away and notified Chen Jinrong of the divorce with a lawyer's letter. Jinrong did not show weakness and hired a lawyer to deal with it. He learned that his elder brother, Chen Jinwen, and Chen Ni were hiding in the Central Apartments on Kaizi Road, Eight Immortals Bridge, first in room number 2, then in room number 20. He reported it to the police with his lawyer, Zhang Shiying, and had Chen Jinwen and Chen Ni arrested and detained in the local court. At the same time, a pair of love letters written by Chen Jinwen were seized and attached to the file. The prosecutor cited Article 239 and Article 240, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law to indict them. Yesterday, Judge Wu Xiangzu opened the trial. The defendants denied adultery, but claimed that Ni had been abused by her husband and asked lawyer Zhang Bao to write a letter notifying him of the divorce. Chen Jinwen claimed that he was acting on his father's orders to go and reconcile them, and happened to meet Ni in front of the Central Apartments, so he advised her. He did not expect to be arrested, etc. Their father, Chen Caiyuan, testified in court that he knew nothing about his elder son's adultery with his younger daughter-in-law. Chen Jinrong testified that this was proven by Zhang Shiying's lawyer who went with him to arrest them. The love letter seized was written by his elder brother. However, he and his brother were half-brothers. Now that his father and relatives have come to mediate, he requested that they be allowed bail first, and they would withdraw the charges after the conditions were agreed upon. The judge, however, reasoned that there was no such free and convenient way to first grant bail and then discuss conditions when a lawsuit was involved. Therefore, he ruled that bail was not allowed. The case was adjourned for further hearing, and the defendants were returned to custody.

Fei Xiuzhen's Case Against Her Paramour Resolved; Court Rules Case Not Accepted

Fei Xiuzhen, a local woman aged 30, was married to Pan Yuelu, a teacher, and had several children. After Pan died four years ago, Fei, unwilling to remain a widow, became acquainted with Li Chengyuan, a former employee of the Lianglu Road Bureau from Yangzhou, last year, and cohabited with him at 36 Xinxingli, North Sichuan Road. After the death of Fei's late husband, she inherited a considerable amount of property. After she began cohabiting with Li, Li used the pretext of starting a business and borrowed a total of 5,700 yuan from Fei, all with written IOUs. Recently, Li's father became acquainted with a prostitute named Xiuqin Lao Jiu from the Fuxiangli brothel on Guangxi Road, leading to frequent conflicts between Fei and Li. On the 27th of last month, Fei went to Xiuqin's place to negotiate with Li. After a brief conflict, Fei did not return home that evening. Li then secretly returned and stole the written IOUs and other items and fled. Fei reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, and Chinese detective Liu Zhaonian arrested Li and handed him over to the First Special District Court. Li claimed that he and Fei had held a wedding ceremony and had a marriage certificate. The court stated that further investigation was needed and announced that the case would be adjourned, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, this case was further heard by Judge Zhan Liangce in the Criminal Court No. 5. The police lawyer, Jiang Baolian, stated that, according to reports, the plaintiff and defendant had reached a settlement during the adjournment period, with Li Chengyuan writing seven additional IOUs to Fei. However, this further proved the defendant's criminal behavior. Next, Fei's lawyer, Fan Gang, stated that the case had been resolved and requested that the complaint be withdrawn. After Judge Zhan reviewed the IOUs written by Li and confirmed that they were in his own handwriting, he ruled that the case would not be accepted.

New Bride Commits Suicide After Failing to Get Watch and Coat

Ling Meimei, a 19-year-old granddaughter of the late Ling Fusheng, who lived next to the Public Security Bureau in Niheng Lane, Gaoqiao Town, Pudong, was not unattractive but was usually taciturn and focused on her needlework. Her parents died early, and she was raised by her grandmother. Through a matchmaker, she was betrothed to a man named someone from Chuansha Township and was scheduled to marry in November. The groom's family sent betrothal gifts worth 300 yuan, and her aunt helped prepare her dowry, which cost a total of 500 yuan. However, Meimei still wanted to buy a watch and coat, but her aunt refused, and she became despondent. She bought a piece of opium somewhere and secretly swallowed it the night before. Around midnight, the poison took effect, and she groaned in bed. Her grandmother discovered it and immediately took her to the hospital set up by the Health Bureau. The doctor gave her an injection, but it was too late. She was taken back home and died. The Public Security Bureau ordered the local headman, Shen Guanfu, to report it to the local court, which sent a prosecutor and coroner by boat to the town to examine the body and ordered the family to prepare the coffin.

The "Shibao" Workers Union Sends a Letter Regarding the Ge Case, Requesting the Swift Arrest of the Brother-in-Law and Adulteress

Yesterday, the "Shibao" factory affairs council, regarding the Ge case, specially petitioned the Shanghai Newspaper Industry Workers Union to strictly arrest the murderer. The document stated, "Concerning the murder of a husband by a murderer who is at large, we implore you to forward this to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for the swift arrest of the criminals to uphold human life. Our union member Ge Guanfu, a worker at 'Shenbao', was fatally attacked in his residence in Sanduoli on the 13th of this month by his brother-in-law, Lin, and his adulterous wife, Liu Xiangbao, who severed his neck with a kitchen knife, causing immediate death. The murderers are at large and have not yet been apprehended. If they are allowed to roam free for a long time, not only will the deceased hold a grudge in the afterlife, but all union workers, due to our camaraderie, will feel ashamed towards our deceased fellow worker. Therefore, we specially petition your union to promptly forward this to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, ordering its subordinates to swiftly arrest the adulterer and adulteress, ensuring that none escape the net, so that they can be brought to justice as soon as possible and sentenced to capital punishment. This will not only console our deceased friend in the afterlife but also slightly alleviate the indignation of all union workers. Submitted urgently, we remain at your service. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Newspaper Industry Workers Union, "Shibao" Factory Affairs Council, October 18th."

After a Quarrel with Her Husband, a Young Woman Swallows a Gold Ring

Wang Lindi, a woman from Wuxi, aged 25, living at 16 Jukang Street in the Nanshi district, had a quarrel with her husband over a minor matter yesterday morning. Unexpectedly, after her husband went out, Lindi angrily swallowed a gold ring, intending to end her life. Her family discovered it and rushed her to the hospital for treatment. After the doctor gave her an enema and injection, it had not been expelled as of last night.

Thieves Rob Military Officer of Clothes; Arrested After Discovery, Police Called for Investigation

Ma Zhengping, from Henan, aged 23, a junior officer in a certain division, was recently discharged and came to Shanghai by boat, intending to return to his hometown. Unexpectedly, when he disembarked at the 16th Pier the night before last, his clothes and luggage were robbed by pier looters led by Huang Decheng. He searched for them without success and reported it to the police. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, he suddenly encountered the robbers at the entrance of Baodai Lane. He immediately apprehended them and questioned them about the robbery, but they were evasive. He then took them to various places to search. At a small teahouse on Xinkaihe Road, he saw members of the gang, Wang Afu and Chen Wenbin, drinking tea at the same table. Next to the table were leather shoes and a coat. Ma saw that they were his belongings and immediately called the police, who arrested Wang, Chen, and their leader, Huang Decheng, and took them to the Yemiao Police Station for investigation. After interrogation, it was learned that the defendants had been robbing travelers at the pier for some time, and their actions were extremely illegal. They were handed over to the bureau for legal action.

Renting Out Remaining Rooms is Risky; Three Thieves Pretend to View and Rob

There was a upstairs in Tongchangli, 50 Haining Road, for rent. At 9:30 a.m. yesterday, three men in Western suits knocked on the door and claimed they wanted to see the house. They barged into the inner room and took out handguns, scaring everyone into silence. They robbed over 200 yuan in legal tender and fled. Afterward, the landlord reported it to the police station for investigation.

Two Thieves Lure People to Gamble and Steal Their Money

Chai Mishun, from Ningbo, aged 35, opened a cigarette and paper shop at 63 Yangshupu Road. Yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., he passed by Xinkaihe Road on business. There, he saw local robbers Fang Fusheng, Sun Ajui, and others setting up a "flower leaf" gambling stall on the roadside. Seeing that Chai was naive, they lured him to gamble. Chai happened to stop and watch, and the robbers accused him of not paying his losses, forcibly seizing 15 yuan in legal tender from him and beating him before fleeing. Chai chased them to Danfeng Road and called police officer Tian Ziliang, who intercepted the two robbers, Fang and Sun, and took them to the Yemiao Police Station for investigation. After interrogation, it was learned that the defendants had been luring people to gamble and stealing their money. Their actions were extremely illegal. They were handed over to the bureau for strict handling.

Southern Huangpu: Flour Boat Encountered Thieves

A flour boat captained by Liu Genbao was carrying 500 bags of wheat bran powder to Songjiang the other day. Yesterday morning at 5 a.m., while sailing at Shibali in Southern Huangpu, several small boats suddenly approached. Inside were more than a dozen thieves armed with sharp knives and iron rods. Three of the thieves were wearing broken yellow military uniforms. They swarmed onto the boat, beat Liu, and demanded that he hand over his money. He replied that there was no money on the boat, so they tied him and his five crew members with ropes. Seeing the situation was dire, they did not dare to resist and allowed them to search. Liu's wife, Fang, seeing the situation, hid in the back cabin, wrapped the money and two gold rings she had in a package, and hid them under the flour sacks. When the thieves searched the cabin, they found nothing. They had no choice but to rob all the clothes and bedding from the boat and carry away more than a dozen bags of flour before fleeing.

Continued Arrest of Accomplices in the Cold Rice Struggle Murder Case; Held Awaiting Joint Trial with Lu Caifa

The North and South cold rice ruffians, on the evening of the 8th of this month at 11 p.m., gathered dozens of people each, wielding knives, sticks, and other weapons, engaging in a battle near Qiwupu Road, Huade Road. As a result, Gao Liansheng, a man from Lu, was slashed in the head with a knife and died. Chinese detective Jin Guanya of Yulin Road and Chinese officers 2486 and 2437 apprehended three accomplices: Lu Caifa from Yong, and Wang Songting from Anhui, as well as the deceased's younger brother, Gao Lianming. They were taken to the police station along with a large knife and a nail-toothed wooden stick that had been discarded, and handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. It has been reported that another accomplice, Bao Jinbao from Tongzhou, was subsequently arrested and sent to the hospital for detention. At 3:30 a.m. the day before yesterday, Chinese officer 1579 arrested the leader of the South, Huang Jinfa (also known as Xiao Hei Tan), from Pudong on East Broadway. He was sent to Criminal Court No. 3 yesterday morning, where Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the investigation. The Municipal Council lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, explained the previous situation and stated that after the defendant was arrested, they learned that the leaders Xiao Baiyan and Pudong Ma Pi were either lingering near the China Merchants Bureau Wharf in the French Concession. Chinese and Western detectives went to arrest them but were unable to find them. They also checked 32 Sanguantang Lane, Huaji Road, but they were not there either. It was requested that the case be adjourned for a joint trial with Lu Caifa and others. When questioned, Huang Jinfa confessed that he was a cold rice worker and that Pudong Ma Pi had invited him to fight there. The nail-toothed wooden root was held by the other side, the northern men, and was seized by us. He did not know about Xiao Baiyan's proposal to exchange contracts with the northern gang leaders and the plan for both gangs to go to Zhabei to rob property while residents were moving. Judge Xiao ruled for remand and adjourned the case for a joint trial and detention with Lu Caifa.

Fire Sparks from Celluloid Shavings Along the Wall

Along the section of Minzhu Street, Fuyou Road in the Shanghai city, celluloid shops (that is, celluloid) are lined up. The shop staff often dump celluloid shavings at the foot of the wall at the intersection, piled up like hills. Celluloid is most easily flammable. Yesterday (the 19th) at 12:45 a.m., a fire started when a pedestrian threw a leftover cigarette butt into the pile of celluloid shavings. The fire flared up instantly, and the flames were so fierce that they could not be approached, causing the bamboo curtains of the Weisheng South Goods Shop at No. 61 to ignite. Fortunately, the shop staff managed to put out the fire. By the time the fire trucks from various districts arrived, the smoke had long since dissipated.

Demanding Old Debt, Creditor Wounded with Knife

Zhu Bi, a woman from Yancheng, aged 45, makes a living by lending money at high interest rates. She lives in a bungalow on Zhangjia Road, Zhabei. During the winter of last year, Shen Jingui, a peddler from Funing, borrowed five yuan from her, promising to pay back two jiao in silver dollars per day, including principal and interest. However, Shen only paid back a little over ten jiao and then disappeared. It wasn't until yesterday afternoon at around 4 p.m. that Zhu Bi finally found him. When she demanded the old debt, a verbal conflict ensued. Shen became enraged and stabbed Zhu Bi in the right cheek with a small knife, causing profuse bleeding. The police officer who saw it took them both to the station for questioning.

Robbery in Caojiazhai, West Shanghai

At 6:30 p.m. the night before last, four robbers suddenly came to the home of Yao Enrong, a local resident living at 11 Xinglianfang, Nan Caojiazhai, Jixifeier Road, West Shanghai. The robbers were wearing blue cloth short-sleeved shirts and trousers and spoke with a Jiangbei accent. Two of the robbers each held a handgun, scaring everyone into silence. They robbed Yao of a gold ring on his hand and nine yuan in silver dollars and fled in different directions. Yao immediately reported it to the Caojadu Public Security Sub-bureau and requested an investigation.

Carelessness at the Great Wall Pencil Factory; Losses Still Small

At around 9 a.m. yesterday, while work was in progress, a fire suddenly broke out in the drying room of the Great Wall Pencil Factory at 223 Shen'anli, Labourte Road, West Shanghai. The Caojadu Fire Brigade was immediately notified and dispatched a fire engine to put out the fire. It was extinguished at 9:30 a.m. It is reported that the factory's losses were still small.

Wang Yansong's Mother Passes Away; Condolences Sent from All Sectors

After the mother of Wang Yansong, a member of the Central People's Training Committee, passed away in his hometown, relatives and friends from all sectors in Beijing and Shanghai sent telegrams of condolence. Madam Wang was placed in a coffin on the 17th (the day before yesterday). The telegrams of condolence from all sectors are compiled below: "To Mr. Wang Yansong, Wan Shi Cun, I am deeply saddened by the passing of your respected mother. Please take care of yourself. I send you this telegram of condolence. Chen Qicai, Tang Naikang, salute." "To Brothers Wang Yansong and Wang Yankang, Wan Shi Cun, Madam has completed her life and has no regrets. I hope you will restrain your grief to assist in important matters. Zhuang Yunqing, Fang Jiao, Bo Gu, Xin Yi, Wan Jiechen, Tu Kaizheng, Shen Xuewen, salute." "To Mr. Wang Yansong and Wang Yankang, Wan Shi Cun, Madam has passed away. I am deeply saddened. Please take care of yourself and turn your grief into strength to assist in important matters. Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Standing Committee Members Du Yuesheng, Xu Jilun, Jin Runxiang, Ke Ganchen, salute." "To Brothers Wang Yansong and Wang Yankang, Wan Shi Cun, I am saddened to learn of Madam's passing. As I am far away, I cannot attend the funeral in person. I send you this telegram of condolence. I hope you will take care of yourself. Wen Lanting, Chen Ziming, Zhang Peizhen, Yang Guanbei, Zhu Wenqi, salute." "To Brother Wang Yansong, Wan Shi Cun, I am saddened to learn of Madam's passing. Please take care of yourself and turn your grief into strength to assist in important matters. I pray for you and send you this telegram of condolence. Your brother, Pan Gongzhan, salute." "To Mr. Wang Yansong, I am deeply saddened by the passing of your mother. The news has deeply saddened us. Please take care of yourself and turn your grief into strength to assist in important matters. We send you this telegram of condolence. The Shanghai Silk Industry Association, salute." "To Mr. Wang Yansong and Wang Yankang, I am shocked and saddened to learn of Madam's sudden passing. I send you this telegram of condolence. Lu Zidong and Lu Chongzhi of the Silk Industry Bank, with all colleagues, salute."

News of Memorial Gifts for the New Wuzhou Police News Building

The new building of the Wuzhou Pharmacy on Fuzhou Road was opened on the 11th and has been holding a three-week gift-giving event. Because it is in commemoration of this unprecedented event, the gifts are particularly generous. An additional gift of five jiao of this brand's product will be given for every two large bars of Guyuan soap purchased (calculated by multiples of five jiao). If you purchase five yuan of this brand's product, in addition to the twenty bars of Guyuan soap, you will also receive a piggy bank. Gifts are also given for the purchase of other brands' products. Customers can not only see the company's new buildings and equipment but also get particularly generous gifts, so they are spreading the word and flocking to the store. The front of the new Wuzhou building is often unbearably crowded.

Shanghai Dinghai Fellow Association: Second Expanded Dinner Party; Very Enthusiastic Attendance

The Dinghai Fellow Association of Shanghai held its second expanded dinner party at the Atlantic Western Restaurant on the 17th of this month to promote fellowship among the hometown community. The attendance was very enthusiastic, with over a hundred hometown residents attending, making it a grand occasion. It is reported that during the dinner, fellow residents proposed that family members of the members be invited to participate in the third expanded dinner party, and that music and other entertainment would be held after the dinner.

Songjiang Fellow Association: Yesterday's Inaugural Meeting

Since its planning, the Songjiang Fellow Association of Shanghai has been progressing smoothly. It has already been approved by the Municipal Party Department and issued a permit for filing. Yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., the inaugural meeting was held at 735 Fuxu Road. More than thirty people attended. Chairman Zhang Xiaotong recorded the meeting, and Hu Tiansheng gave a brief report on the purpose of the meeting, stating, "Although there was an organization of Songjiang fellow residents in Shanghai before, it was only a gathering for leisure and entertainment for the idle class, and it soon disappeared. We, recognizing the need for collective solidarity among fellow residents, are launching an organized fellow association. On the one hand, we will enable fellow residents to connect and solve all the difficulties faced by fellow residents in Shanghai. On the other hand, we aim to use human and financial resources to promote the prosperity of our hometown. We aim to implement this in the initial two-year period. If we can lay the foundation and achieve significant results, the future prospects are unlimited," etc. It was decided that Xu Gongmei, Geng Ji Zhi, etc., would successively express their opinions and sincerely promote the progress of the association. The preparatory committee members Wu Kaixian, Ma Yinliang, Geng Ji Zhi, Zhang Xiaotong, Wu Xiu, Zhang Renchun, Song Chuanji, Gu Shisheng, Cai Buzi, Pang Mingsan, Zhu Wenxin, Hu Tiansheng, Dong Changqiu, Xu Gongmei, Xu Zhongming, Qi Guangdi, Shen Yijun, Zhu Mingxin, and Shen Liangzhong, nineteen in total, were appointed. It was decided to hold the first preparatory meeting next week to actively solicit members. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Newly Published: An Introduction to Paper Money

Jiang Tingfu, a senior staff member of the Four Banks Savings Society, has recently authored a book titled "An Introduction to Paper Money." The content is divided into two parts, upper and lower, comprising a total of twenty chapters. It offers a detailed exposition on the knowledge of paper money. The upper part covers theory and practice, with content regarding theory first providing a detailed explanation of the meaning, nature, and types of paper money, followed by a detailed discussion of the advantages and disadvantages of paper money, its issuance, reserve, exchange, and the various theories of paper money held by scholars from different countries. The practical aspects cover the manufacturing, destruction, and accounting of paper money, all based on academic principles and experience, with detailed descriptions. The chapter on issuance accounting includes various sample account forms. The lower part provides a systematic record of the origin of paper money and the history of issuance in various countries, with detailed tables listing the number and year of issuance from the beginning to the most recent. The situation of various historical and current issuances in our country is recorded in detail. Finally, various issuance regulations and laws of our country over the years are compiled at the end as an appendix for easy reference. The book is printed by Zhonghua Book Company and is now available. The price is set at 90 cents per copy, with a 30% discount for purchases made within this year.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated: sunny and rather cool around Shandong, the Yellow River basin, and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River, with southwest to northwest winds; morning fog in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, with strong northwest to north winds; cloudy to overcast with rain in the East China Sea and Taiwan, with very strong northeast to northwest winds; cyclones and bad weather in the southern part of Kyushu, caused by the typhoon east of Naha moving northeast-north or northeast; a low-pressure area has formed southeast of Yap Island, and the center of the typhoon moved to within 60 miles of 27 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, with fierce winds. YMCA to Hold Winter Heated Swimming

In order to promote winter swimming, the YMCA has specially organized a heated swimming session, which has already started registration. The details are summarized as follows:

Regulations

(1) Origin: In order to promote swimming, the association will continue to organize heated swimming sessions, so that those who can swim will not be interrupted by the season, affecting their progress, and those who cannot swim will have the opportunity to participate in practice at any time. (2) Qualifications: (A) Members of the association, (B) Those introduced by members of the association, (C) Schools and organizations (more than 15 people), (D) Female school students. (3) The opening period for this season is from November 1 of this year to the end of April next year. (4) Membership fees: (A) Members of the association: (a) 10 yuan for the whole season, (b) 2 yuan per month. (B) Junior members: 5 yuan for the whole season, three hours (three times) per week. (C) Non-members: (a) 20 yuan for the whole season, (b) 4 yuan per month. (D) Schools and organizations: (a) 6 yuan for the whole season, two hours (twice) per week, (b) 8 yuan for the whole season, three hours (three times) per week. (E) Female school students: 6 yuan for the whole season, two hours (twice) per week. (5) Opening hours for each class: (A) General class: Monday to Saturday, 12:00 PM to 2:00 PM, Monday to Saturday 5:30 PM to 7:00 PM. (B) Beginner class: Monday and Thursday, 8:00 PM to 9:00 PM. (C) Junior members: Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM. (D) Women's class: Wednesday, 4:30 PM to 5:30 PM, Saturday, 3:00 PM to 4:00 PM. The time for other school organizations will be determined separately.

Rules

(1) All swimmers must have their physical condition examined by a doctor designated by the association (other doctors must be approved by the association) and obtain a permit before they can participate in swimming. (2) Swimmers, men do not need to wear swimming suits, and women must wear hats in addition to clothing. (3) Swimmers must enter and exit according to the prescribed time. When they come, they must exchange their swimming certificate for a towel and a locker key. The certificate must not be lent to others. Once found, it will be cancelled immediately. (4) Swimmers must take a shower before swimming. No behavior that hinders public health is allowed in or beside the pool. (5) If anyone violates the above rules and does not listen to warnings, the association has the right to cancel their swimming privileges and the membership fee will not be refunded.

Reflections on Inspecting European Sports (Part 1)

— Jiang Lianggui

(Berlin Correspondence) The 11th World Games were held in Berlin. In addition to sending a large delegation, the Sports Advancement Association of our country also organized a sports inspection team, selecting service personnel from the national sports community to come to Europe to participate in the World Games, and after the closing of the Games, went to various European countries with special history or achievements in sports for inspection, lasting a total of 18 days, visiting seven countries including Denmark, Sweden, Czech Republic, Hungary, Italy, Austria, and Germany. The scope of the inspection included social sports, school sports, and other organizations such as youth training and labor service groups. I, as a reporter, was very honored to follow the gentlemen of the sports community to visit together. It is a pity that the time was too short, and there was no lack of regret for a cursory glance. Detailed inspection notes have been sent to the country in each country's journey, but what is described are some descriptions of the actual situation, lacking personal subjective criticism and feelings. Therefore, I specially write a little bit about the feelings and solutions to the questions that were previously considered doubtful, gained from this inspection. Although the sports of each country have their different social backgrounds and political propositions, we cannot judge what to copy them all, but on the whole, it can be used as a reference from other mountains.

(1) The Position of Physical Education in the School Curriculum

This is a consistent proposition and principle in any country. Whether we go to a fascist country or a democratic country, in the regulations promulgated by their Ministry of Education, there is always a clause saying "Physical education should occupy the first place in all courses in schools at all levels." Not long ago, the German Ministry of Education also recently promulgated a law stating that "Physical education is an important lesson in university coursework, and students with poor physical education grades will be given a grade retention or expulsion punishment." When this law was first promulgated, it was strongly opposed by some well-known people in society, but later, after careful testing and on-site investigation by the Ministry of Education, objective facts were used to prove that "Students with excellent physical education grades also have excellent academic grades." Therefore, the German Ministry of Education later explained that this measure not only does not affect the progress of science, but directly promotes it, and a group of opposing professors no longer grumble. Therefore, from this point of view, the emphasis on school physical education in Europe is a kind of national policy. Let's take a look at the school physical education situation in China. Anyone who pays a little attention to physical education knows that it is "bankrupt," "failed," and "equal to zero." The physical education in primary schools is, at most, one or two hours of pace, freehand exercises, and games per week. Providing children who are in the rising age of development with one or two hours of exercise per week is undoubtedly very little. What's more, there is a group of derelict physical education teachers who use this only one or two hours to shout a few "one two one" and turn left and right, and just perfunctorily pass it off. This is simply not education, this is destroying children, this is harming the health of the entire nation. Let's talk about middle school, it's even more messy. Students are called in absentia or simply don't have it. If there are a few schools that are serious about physical education, it is very pitiful, truly rare. Speaking of university, it can be said that there is none at all. What is the so-called university physical education in China now? At most, it is just university interscholastic competitions? Each school has a football team and a basketball team, and they often come out to play a few games. Those who can get the championship are successful. The general students, at least 90% or more, have nothing to do with physical education. Although the Ministry of Education has repeatedly emphasized that "Entrance physical education should be included in regular classes," the result is that thorough implementation is of course out of the question, and even perfunctory compliance is not seen. Therefore, we see that a young person, from elementary school to university, the physique built in this kind of physical education environment cannot be morbid and weak. Perhaps there are a few sports enthusiasts in the school, and the result is the formation of a special class, only exercising and not studying. These morbidities and crises in school physical education naturally directly and indirectly contain countless factors, and the result of their interaction and evolution. However, I believe that the biggest problem, the most severe impact, is "the unimportant position of physical education in various courses." Because it is not important, physical education teachers have no status, physical education courses are not paid attention to, physical education funds are reduced and misappropriated, physical education grades are insignificant, and all kinds of malpractices are numerous. Therefore, we hope, we want to shout loudly, you people who run education, your responsibility is "to create perfect children, but you unconsciously what you have done in the past is to destroy children, to harm children, if you want to achieve your goals, to fulfill your responsibilities, you must change your past erroneous views, educate children, put physical education on the front line, make full use of it, and give full play to the value of physical education in education, and turn around quickly in this way, perhaps it can still be remedied and recovered in case of emergency.

(2) The Question of Differences and Similarities Between Male and Female Physical Education This question gave me a satisfactory answer during this inspection process. From observations in various aspects, and the results of inquiries with famous figures in the sports world in various countries, the conclusion we have reached is "Male and female physical education, in principle, can adopt the same training methods." We have seen many women whose activities and abilities in sports are not lower than men's. Originally, men and women have the same ability to survive and should enjoy equal training opportunities. The mistake of the past was that women's physical strength was thought to be weaker than men's, so physical activities should be different from men's. This is a fundamental mistake. You must know that the decline in women's physical fitness is by no means a morbidity, but a normal state. There are probably two reasons for the decline in women's physical fitness: A. Historical factors Because since human history, men have always been the center of society, and women have always been in a subordinate position, so women are always the protected and supported. The competition of life and the acquisition of food and clothing are all the sole responsibility of men. Since women do not need to operate, the opportunity for instinctive activities is reduced, so gradually evolved, and the physical fitness naturally gradually declined. Therefore, the decline in women's physical fitness is not an instinctive tendency, but the result of being influenced by history. If we continue to not give women appropriate activities, then in the future, perhaps women will not even be able to walk.

B. Physiological Factors The second reason is physiological. The physiological factors that most affect women's physical fitness are the lowering of the center of gravity. Women have a larger pelvis in preparation for childbirth, so the weight of the lower part increases, the center of gravity lowers, and action is inconvenient. At the same time, the pelvis expands, and the inclination of the legs also increases, making it difficult to swing. In addition, such as more fat, high specific gravity, loose muscles, etc., are all physiological factors that affect the ability to exercise.

Therefore, the reason why women's sports performance is not as good as men's and their physical strength is not as good as men's is the result of historical and physiological reasons. In fact, there is no difference in the physique of men and women. They need the same exercise and the same training. Of course, in fact, because of the above two reasons, in the present era, when training women, it must not be the same "amount" as men, but at least we can know that men's and women's physical education are the same in principle."

Ministry of Education Supervisor, Sun Guofeng, Memorial Record

The memorial service for Ministry of Education Supervisor Sun Guofeng was solemnly held at 9 a.m. on the 18th in the main auditorium of the Ministry of Education. In attendance were Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education, Division Chief Duan, along with bureau directors, secretaries, counselors, specialists, supervisors, and many other staff members from various divisions and offices, as well as senior officials from other ministries, councils, and the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, the Library, university presidents, provosts, leaders of academic organizations, and others, totaling more than 200 people. At the start of the meeting, everyone stood in solemn silence and bowed three times to Mr. Sun’s portrait. Minister Wang first offered a flower during the memorial ceremony, followed by Jin Yufu reading the eulogy. Next, Duan Xipeng, the Director of Educational Affairs, reported on Supervisor Sun’s work at the Ministry of Education and the course of his illness caused by overwork. Zhuang Changgong reported on Sun's diligence and achievements during his tenure at Northeastern University. Ding Xu reported on Sun's diligent study and thoughtful spirit during his time studying in the United States. Finally, Minister Wang reported that Supervisor Sun's inspection area was particularly broad during his time as a higher education inspector, and that he made many contributions based on his observations during the inspection, which greatly improved higher education. Today, looking at his portrait, not only are we personally saddened, but also as a public servant with specialized knowledge, loyalty, sincerity, and a willingness to work hard, we should mourn the loss of talent to the public. Mr. Sun was upright and his family was destitute. Efforts should be made to provide relief through public and private means. After the report, a group photo was taken and the meeting adjourned. The venue was decorated with wreaths (from the Capital Memorial Service, the Nanjing Peking University Alumni Association, etc.) and elegiac couplets (from Zhuang Changgong, Su Shangda, Shen Qixun, Zhao Yuchang, Wang Xuehai, Cui Shunqing, etc.). Among them, the couplet jointly offered by the colleagues of the Capital Memorial Service was the most detailed and comprehensive, and also expressed regret and sorrow. The lyrics said, "He was versatile and talented throughout his life, specializing in engineering and science, and was early on expected to select elites and cultivate people. Now that the national crisis is at its height, how could it be that the horse herd is empty in Hebei?" "He was diligent and courageous in his duties, and his virtue was suddenly lost. Even if only the cold wind of Zhongfu remains, and the moon of Yantai is cold, thinking of his homeland in sight, we still expect him to transform into a crane and return to Liaodong." Now, Mr. Sun's brief biography is recorded below:

Brief Biography of Sun Guofeng: Mr. Sun's name was Guofeng, his courtesy name was Xianting, and his surname was Sun. He was a native of Changtu County, Liaoning Province. In his youth, he entered the provincial middle school, then transferred to a higher school, and then ascended to Peking University, where he studied physics. He always topped his class in every exam. After completing his studies, he stayed at the school as a teaching assistant. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, he passed the first higher civil service examination and was assigned to work in the Ministry of the Navy. Mr. Sun was not satisfied with this, so he went to the United States to study at Cornell University, still studying physics. After a long time, he obtained a doctorate degree and worked for an electric power company in a certain province, where he made many inventions. He returned after several years. At that time, the authorities in the Eastern Provinces were preparing to establish Northeastern University in Shenyang, and he was appointed as the Dean of Science. Later, the department was changed to a college, and he served as the Dean of the College of Science and Engineering for eight years. The students he cultivated numbered in the thousands, and they all happily left according to their wishes. In the autumn of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, Mr. Sun had just resigned from his position at the university when the Shenyang Incident suddenly occurred. He went through the pass alone, wanting to save the situation, but to no avail. He then took the position of Dean of the College of Engineering at Peiping University. After more than a year, he was unhappy and resigned. Soon after, he was appointed as a specialist in the Ministry of Education and then received the order of supervisor, serving in the capital. Every year, he went to various provinces and cities to inspect schools above the specialist level, often traveling thousands of miles. When he returned, he worked on reports at his desk, without a single day of rest throughout the year. And Mr. Sun's illness was already lurking at this time. This summer, Mr. Sun was ordered to go to eastern Guangdong to inspect educational affairs. He braved the heat and traveled quickly. After more than a month of service, he returned and suffered from thirst and a fondness for eating melons, and also suffered from a sore throat. He went to Peiping for medical treatment. Later, he developed a fever and difficulty swallowing. The doctor diagnosed him with acute pneumonia. In just five or six days, he died at Shou Shan Hospital, on September 27 of the 25th year. Mr. Sun was calm and open-minded, and deeply thoughtful. He once said that he was healthy, so he was brave in taking on responsibilities, but in the end, he fell ill and died because of this. He died at the age of forty-eight. He had one son and two daughters. His son died three years ago, at the age of eight. Mr. Sun was also unhappy because of this. He was not good at accumulating wealth in his life, so there was no remaining savings after his death. All those who knew him said that he was in his prime and had not yet completed his achievements. When they heard that he had died of illness, they could not help but shed tears.

Municipal People's Education Center and Library Merged

The sites of the Municipal People's Education Center and the Municipal Library are both located in the Confucian Temple on Confucian Temple Road, Ximen. Over the years, both institutions have achieved considerable success in providing public education. Recently, after the merger of the two bureaus of social education, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in order to adjust subordinate institutions and save expenses, has obtained the approval of the Municipal Government to order the merger and reorganization of the two institutions, and to appoint Xu Zexiang, the current director of the Municipal Library and supervisor of the bureau, as the director of the People's Education Center. Upon receiving the order, Mr. Xu closed the Municipal Library on October 1st and took over the People's Education Teachers. Recently, the internal affairs of the center have been sorted out, and efforts are being made to develop and improve the business aspects, such as the national martial arts team, morning exercise team, singing team, reading club, public school, children's library, consumer cooperative, public medical consultation, public knowledge guidance, broadcasting lectures, etc. It is also heard that after the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau ordered the abolition of the Municipal National Goods Exhibition Hall, all the national goods exhibits will also be transferred to the People's Education Center for display and safekeeping. Therefore, in addition to expanding the original exhibition rooms for hygiene and science, the center is also planning to add a national goods exhibition room.

Zhejiang University Added Academic Inquiry Office Approved by the Ministry of Education

Zhejiang University approved the letter from the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education to send the resolution of the eighth meeting of the primary school conference office this spring, "Requesting that a letter be transferred to Zhejiang Da Bi to establish an academic inquiry office." The reason for this is that "educational science has a very close relationship with other academic disciplines. Therefore, Thorndike said that those engaged in education must have broad knowledge in order to cope with it easily. However, academic progress is constantly innovating, and primary school teachers' knowledge acquired during school education in the past is not enough to cope with the new environment. Even if they can read newspapers and magazines to make up for it, it is still difficult to find the necessary materials at times. Therefore, it is necessary to wait for inquiries. If a national university can establish an inquiry mechanism so that letters can be sent for inquiries, then there will be a way to seek advice, and difficulties can be solved." The Zhejiang University authorities believe that this theory is quite insightful, and the school affairs meeting decided to temporarily pilot it through the Academic Affairs Office, but it is limited to correspondence inquiries, that is, designating staff members of the teaching office to handle the receiving, sending, and sorting of these inquiry letters. All those outside the school who are interested in research can send academic questions directly to the school's Academic Inquiry Office. The office can then present them to the Dean of Academic Affairs nearby and forward them to the relevant department's professors for research and reply. It has expanded the scope and is not limited to primary school teachers. The brief outline of the office is appended below: 1. The university's affiliated academic inquiry office is for correspondence inquiries from outside the school on academic issues. 2. This inquiry is temporarily limited to correspondence inquiries. 3. All inquiries are limited to those with academic research value. 4. After receiving the questions, the office will submit them to the Dean of Academic Affairs and forward them to the professors of the relevant departments for reply. 5. All questions raised must describe the origins in detail for research purposes. 6. Incoming letters must be written clearly. 7. Incoming letters must include postage for registered mail for return. 8. If the reply to the questions raised is quite complicated, the office may charge a fee at its discretion. 9. Questions that do not meet the above rules will not be answered.

The Publicity of the Achievement of the Scout Inspection Has Aroused Dissatisfaction in the Municipal Scout Community, and a Telegram Has Been Sent to the General Association to Investigate the Truth

Guomin News Agency reported that the National Boy Scout Inspection and Camping was held in Beijing around the Double Tenth Festival. The details have already been recorded in this newspaper. The scores and comments of the representative teams from various places were slightly published in various newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai on the 16th. However, the Scout General Association officially corrected the reports to various newspapers the next day, believing that the published scores were not factual. According to the person in charge of the Municipal Boy Scout Council, the reporter of Guomin News Agency said, "When the municipal representative team went to Beijing, the campsite newspaper organized by the conference had defamatory remarks about the municipal scouts, fabricating facts and arbitrarily issuing comments, and published them in various newspapers in Beijing. Afterwards, it published unofficial total scores in newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai, and noted that "Shanghai's performance was the worst." Although the news was officially corrected by the General Association, there must be a small number of unscrupulous people using written publicity with the intention of destroying the city's real military undertakings. According to the municipal Boy Scout Council, although the designated camp area was very narrow when the municipal Boy Scouts participated in the conference in Beijing this time, and could not fully provide suitable use for campsite life, all equipment and arrangements were operated by the scouts themselves. Although we dare not boast that the various achievements are good, we are confident that they will not be the worst." It is also known that the Municipal Boy Scout Council has telegraphed the General Association yesterday to ask them to thoroughly investigate the person in charge of publishing inaccurate scores, so as not to confuse the public.

The fuel category index fell by 0.5%, which was due to the slight drop in the retail price of kerosene.

The monthly indexes of various categories are compared with the indexes of the previous month and the same month last year in the table below.
