Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Xiao Bai)

The city is a melting pot of human life. All the skyscrapers, foreign houses, cars, criminal courts, police, exchanges, clubs, dance halls, brothels, red pill sales offices, large gambling dens, etc... it has created people, and it has also killed people. It is hated by people, but it is also praised by people.

The countryside is the source of human life materials. All the rice grains, wheat, vegetables, fruits, silk, cotton, etc. come from this place. It provides food and clothing for all mankind. It is the foundation of human life, but now it is plagued by famine everywhere, and it is even forgotten by the people in the city.

We are fantasizing that one day, we will coordinate and harmonize the symphony of steel, steam, and electricity in the city with everything in the countryside, fundamentally eliminate all the drunkenness, singing, and licentiousness in the city, and completely eliminate all the hunger and cold wastelands in the countryside.

Humanity will begin to live a new and happy life!

Record After Visiting the Family Prototype Exhibition

— Shu Fan

Mr. Zhou Shaofu of Wumen loved skillful crafts during his lifetime. He often studied the art of carving wood and sharpening pits for pleasure. He also liked to travel extensively. When he was a guest in Chengdu, he once saw a set of aprons woven from human bones, inlaid with pearls and emeralds, and as wonderful as brocade weaving. He was delighted with the divine skills of ancient Chinese craftsmanship, which were unattainable. After returning, he increasingly closed his doors and explored, creating in various ways. Later, he felt that it was useless to carve magpies, and it would be easier to make cars and axles for people to understand. So he recruited several craftsmen to work hard for years to supervise the production of household daily utensils, lifelike and carefully imitating the essence. Therefore, within the square area, everything from beds and bedding to tables and cases, calligraphy and paintings, cups and plates, down to dust brooms and chamber pots, could be displayed without leaving anything out. In 1933, he held a pre-exhibition at the Chicago Exposition and won an excellent award certificate. Soon after, Mr. donated the pavilion, and all these wonderful constructions were consigned to dust. Now, his son, Leshan, has slightly reorganized and displayed them all on the fourth floor of Daxin. I have admired them for a long time, and yesterday I was informed that I could enjoy them. They are classified into seven categories: The ancestral hall, where sacrificial vessels are most prominent. The boudoir, where even small items such as jewel boxes are displayed. The hall and the funeral ceremonies are equipped with tools for answering questions and expressing condolences. The Daoist altar and the yacht display the music of Luosheng's banquet and gambling. The school kitchen room is filled with steamers, pots, knives, and chopsticks, which are especially wonderful as if the servants were personally serving. The people sitting, lying, walking, and talking in it are all like their shapes. They are all less than a foot in size, but they are perfectly matched with bean cups and palm tables. Moreover, when carefully examining ceramics, gold, and stone, the inscriptions and engravings are all real. The exquisite craftsmanship of the small objects is amazing. According to the person in charge, the kitchen used to have a cured ham, which was taken from the belly of a pregnant pig, cut off and then made by Dongbai people with potassium nitrate. It was stolen in the farming year, and it is still deeply regretted. In addition, a Daoist scripture in the Daoist altar, with ink as thin as a fly's foot, was also tampered with. To this day, it is difficult to find a skilled hand to fill it. Therefore, I immediately used Lai Zixin as a medium, and Zixin's calligraphy has the skill of placing Mount Sumeru in a mustard seed. I hope that it can complete this wonderful product.

Booksellers' Words

— Tiao Kuang

In order to buy a few books, I happened to walk to Fourth Horse Road and stepped into a Qiming Bookstore. Seeing that their scale was not very large, but it was arranged in a very orderly manner, and the staff was also very friendly; so everyone started talking. In this conversation, there seemed to be a few points that were worth recording!

"Your books are sold so cheaply, isn't this a disguised form of books discounted at 20% off?" I asked.

"It is indeed; but the direction we are taking is different: we do not approve of reprinting those boring novels, but want to promote some new literature; so in this first batch of 30 books issued, which one is not a world literary masterpiece! --What Little Women, Sentimental Education,... a few better books are all included! In addition, there is also a new literary publication, with original novels, dramas, and poems, all of which almost encompass the famous works of recent people!" A young clerk answered as if he were counting family treasures.

"That's very good; then the cost must be very high?"

"The cost is certainly higher; this is not the same as reprinting those boring novels, just taking them and printing them--but we also have our own methods."

"What methods?"

"It's nothing more than reducing expenses to the lowest possible level;" he replied with a smile, "Fortunately, everyone here is young, holding a brave heart, rushing straight forward, how the treatment is, how the working hours are, are not in our hearts, thinking that as long as we do this, we will definitely get a very good result!" He was very generous in guiding here.

"You are willing to do this with all your heart and soul, I think business must be very good?" I couldn't help but compliment him.

"Business is indeed not bad; it's just that because the cost is relatively large and the pricing is low, for example, people can recoup their costs by buying 1,000 copies, but we have to add several times that!—However, we are willing to do this, because at least on the buyer's side, they must be very sympathetic to us!"

I withdrew and thought carefully about this answer, and felt that although there were some elements of self-promotion in it; however, in this era of fierce commercial warfare, this is not a new invention of a business eye, which can be shown to other stores as an example! Therefore, I record it on the right.

Shanghai People's Clothing

— Jiang Gong

"It takes three generations of officials to understand how to dress and eat." This saying shows that in the past, studying beautiful clothes was limited to aristocratic families. Now, it is very different.

In Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, especially in the Suzhou and Hangzhou areas, wearing silk and satin is very common and ordinary, but elsewhere, it is considered a remarkable thing. I remember when I was young and living in Wuchang, I saw with my own eyes that except for officials and wealthy merchants, people rarely wore silk fabrics unless there were weddings, funerals, celebrations, or important banquets. Even wealthy young men, until they were around twenty years old, would be criticized behind their backs for occasionally wearing a fur coat, with people saying, "Aren't they afraid of burning their tender bones!" Even in Beijing, although it has been the capital for many dynasties, the customs of the people were similar. People from places like Shanxi and Shaanxi, who are known for their frugal nature, need no further mention. Look at many important figures from the Northwest, who, despite being in positions of wealth and honor, still wear coarse cloth clothes year-round. This is just their way of doing things and not intentional affectation. The difference between the extravagance and frugality of the North and South is truly immeasurable!

Shanghai people admire vanity the most and love to decorate their appearance. Regardless of their own circumstances or financial resources, they only focus on their clothing, striving to dress themselves in splendid attire, as if they are getting married every day, and everyone is a handsome young man. Even small shop assistants who only earn a dozen yuan a month, poor workers and tea servants, and unemployed vagrants who wander around all day, wear silk from head to toe, inside and out, from their undershirts to the linings of their lined clothes. They would rather go without food than without new clothes, and are willing to borrow money and commit fraud, engage in dishonorable behavior, add to their mental suffering, or even face legal sanctions, all without much care or consideration. "Since ancient times, greedy men have died for wealth, and heroes have died for fame," but Shanghai people only know how to die for clothes. Truly, one crab is worse than another!

However, their policy may be out of necessity, which is not wrong at all. People who want to live in Shanghai really have to do this. Because Shanghai has many vulgar people who are very snobbish and superficial, and they only judge people by their clothes. If you don't have any valuable clothes on, they will look down on you and despise you as worthless!

Common sayings describe people who "swell their faces to look fat" with the phrase "what they wear is on their body, and what they eat is in their belly." But now, Shanghai people are almost the opposite; you could say that "what they eat is on their body, and what they wear is in their belly!" If men are like this, one can imagine what women are like. (According to the news, a young woman committed suicide out of grief because she couldn't get new clothes. This is truly a modern martyr, willing to die for clothes, and her death is heavier than Mount Tai!)

However, in the past few years, new styles of clothing fabrics often sold for four or five yuan a foot, and people still rushed to buy them. Recently, silk and satin have become extremely cheap, and various stores are competing to attract customers with slogans of "unwilling to lose their shirts" and "painful sacrifices." Sacrifice items are sold for only a few cents per foot, but there are few people ordering new clothes. This is not because Shanghai people's enthusiasm for clothing has suddenly decreased. The biggest reason is probably that the public's finances are exhausted and have reached the final stage of "robbing Peter to pay Paul!"

Phoenixes Change Nests

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Brotherly Love Hides a Letter Pitying the Weak Sister; Bookish Air Enters the Shadow, Laughing at the Poor Scholar

Youmei put down her umbrella and sat sideways on a bamboo chair, keeping an eye on Guoguo and Yan Zili. She chatted with Aunt Zhang for a while, but didn't hear any sounds from that room, not even the buzzing of mosquitoes. She thought that Guoguo must not be home. Just then, the maid brought a cup of chrysanthemum tea in a dark green porcelain cup. Youmei took a sip and saw the double dragons playing with pearls on the cup, so she smiled and said, "This must be something Cousin uses. A common person like me would only ruin such an elegant thing." Aunt Zhang sat on the rattan chair opposite her, first glanced at the doorway, then smiled and said to Youmei, "Although he likes everything to be clean and tidy, he doesn't draw any boundaries with people. We only have one bowl of rice to eat now. We were even poorer before, so we really can't afford to look down on anyone, Miss Li, don't you think?" Youmei said, "Of course. Cousin is not only a very good person, but his writing is also so admirable. For example, our classmates see his writing in magazines and discuss him a lot. Some guess correctly, some guess incorrectly, and I find it funny. One person is simply a faithful follower. As long as a magazine has Cousin's writing in it, he will definitely buy it to read." As she said this, there was a "clang" sound from the room. It was clearly the sound of a copper ruler falling on the Xuan paper. Youmei was startled and said, "What? Is Cousin home?" Then she smiled slightly. Aunt Zhang laughed and said, "It doesn't matter if he's home, you didn't say anything bad about him. Don't think that he's been to modern schools since he was young, but he can't be fashionable. He's very generous with men, but he's more timid with women than a girl meeting a man." As Youmei spoke to Aunt Zhang, she looked at the doorway several times and saw a white shadow flickering. She called out, "Cousin is working hard at home! Without your permission, I can't just come into the study to visit." Guoguo replied from inside the room, "I'm sorry. I'm rushing to finish a manuscript, and I'll come out to accompany you when I'm done." Youmei said, "Please do as you please. I'm not a guest, and I have Auntie here to keep me company." Then she turned to Aunt Zhang and whispered, "In this hot weather, he's still shutting himself in his room and being so bookish. He's a bit too steeped in poetry and books." As she spoke, she frowned and smiled wryly. Aunt Zhang laughed and said, "He shouldn't be like this, I always say he's a bookworm." (88)

Random Notes on Autumn

— Wu Jiba

I moved to Caojing over a year ago, and I've been gradually seeing less of my friends in Shanghai. Recently, I've been assisting Mr. Ping, so I've been bustling back and forth between Jing'an and Caojing every day. I happened to realize that the residence of my close friend, Mr. Hu Wenqing, was nearby, so I paid him a visit after work.

Mr. Hu has been managing the Shengde Weaving Factory for many years. He is shrewd, capable, and willing to take responsibility, and is highly relied upon by Mr. Gu Zhaozhen, the factory's owner. Mr. Gu, a native of Suzhou, started a lace business in the downtown area more than twenty years ago. During the European War, foreign goods were cut off, so he raised capital to establish Shengde. Through hard work and careful management, the factory's products became exquisite and sold throughout the country and Southeast Asia within a few years. He further expanded the factory, building a factory base of more than twenty acres on Xiaoshadu Road and adding large-scale machinery, which sped up production and improved quality. It has brought new glory to the national manufacturing industry. The lace produced is constantly updated with new patterns and is even superior to imported goods. Its Sazhen products can also manufacture their own raw materials and distribute them to the Lingzhi Bakelite Instrument Factory, resulting in doubled profits.

In recent years, the market has been sluggish, and the factory has also been affected, but its foundation is solid and it is still able to maintain itself. Recently (starting from October 1st, for a month, as is the usual practice), it held a 22nd-anniversary exhibition to commemorate the founding of the factory. It opened a large room to display various products and offered large discounts to commemorate the occasion. This year, it also cooperated with the Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory to set up displays so that customers could purchase new and unique lace patterns without having to go to the trouble of matching materials. Yesterday, when I visited Mr. Hu, he took me to visit the exhibition hall in the factory. The electric lights were bright, and the colors of the flowers were brilliant. I couldn't take it all in. Among them, the needle department includes weaving, lace weaving, dyeing and other departments, which are managed by Mr. Hu. There is also a Sazhen department, which is a pioneer in the domestic light industry, managed by Mr. Li, also a native of Suzhou. The various bakelite utensils produced are colorful and numerous, and cannot be described in detail. Although the news of the incident had not subsided when I visited, there were still many visitors, especially to see the newly released "Mandarin Duck Lace," which is popular among fashionable partners to trim and embellish their clothes, giving them a unique charm. It is suitable for sales between...

In this time of national crisis, looking at the factories in the country, there are only a few that can manufacture their own raw materials to resist imports. Shengde can stand out and sell more than one million worth of goods a year, which has attracted the attention of foreigners. I hope that those with a will will rise up and revitalize the industry, so I am happy to write about it.

"Salty Water Girl" is a Transliteration

— (Guo Zhenfang)

Yesterday's newspaper said that "salty water girls" are called that because "seawater is salty, and they are doing business at sea, so they are called salty water girls." Although it seems reasonable, it feels like a far-fetched explanation.

As far as I know, "salty water girl" is a transliteration of "Handsome Maid," just like "Delüfeng" (telephone), "Madaka" (car), "Selao Fu" (traveling salesman), and "Kangbaidu" (comprador). It should not be interpreted literally, otherwise, you will get stuck in a dead end.

Special Feature

In the International Cemetery

— Xiafei

Suddenly, I don't know what kind of idea entered my quiet and lonely heart, letting my body drift like a fallen leaf in the autumn wind, aimlessly drifting.

The city under the setting sun is like a magnificent and beautiful oil painting. The arteries of the metropolis are tense and trembling with the heartstrings of the people. On the streets, those people carrying crosses are struggling in this torrent of life as if they have lost their souls!

Many trams, cars, and buses are circling in front of Jing'an Temple like fish in a pond. The three-dimensional architecture and the spiderweb-like wires have already indicated to me that this place has also raised the banner of a prosperous city. Although there is still an ancient Jing'an Temple here, it has not diminished its modern dignity. Now, there are also live plays being performed, crimes being committed, streamlined cars, strugglers on the line of life, haughty gentlemen, unemployed people wandering the streets, rosy dreams, and gray stories... That is a cross-section of Eastern Paris, the edge of Eastern Monte Carlo.

Thinking and walking, I don't know how, by chance, I stumbled into the quiet and solemn International Cemetery.

It is a pure land for the final destination of life. What it suggests to people is only a sense of mystery and liberation. Although no one can avoid entering this final stage, whether they are heroes, beauties, sages, or famous scholars, in the end, they are nothing more than a piece of yellow earth and a pile of white bones. However, after hundreds of years, I think maybe even this piece of yellow earth and a pile of white bones will not be found! Therefore, I feel that setting up these mounds and stone tablets now is unnecessary.

Life is full of contradictions. Some people are always afraid of the arrival of death, but at the same time, some people who think they are smart are constantly digging their own graves. I don't know which of these people is the real fool?

The International Cemetery is a burial ground for people of all nationalities in Shanghai. I believe that the remains of our enemies and the souls of our friends must be buried under these crosses or stone tablets. However, although I have often passed by here before, I have never paid attention to it. Today, I actually stumbled into this place, which is truly a miracle beyond my own expectations.

I love this place very much because it is not only quiet and solemn, but also has extremely elegant and beautiful scenery. The green shade covers the sky, and the soft grass is like a carpet, which makes people linger. Although it is not as well-arranged as a park, with ponds, pavilions, and neatly trimmed flower beds, when we are in it, we can experience a different kind of feeling.

This place is very large, with many stone tablets and crosses standing vertically and horizontally, recording the names of the people. Next to each tomb is a rectangular stone plate filled with pebbles. Some flowers are placed in front of each tomb, and small paths are left on all sides for people to walk. The lush trees are arranged on the sides of the sidewalks, and many unnamed wildflowers are lonely adorned in the middle. In the slanting sunlight and twilight, this group of tombs looks even more desolate and dim.

Walking here alone, I am reminded of the emptiness of life, aware of the loneliness of disillusionment, and it evokes my detached and transcendent view of life. A faint sorrow covers my consciousness like the autumn chill.

Suddenly, a flock of sparrows flew from the trees, chirping and flying among the branches, full of harmonious and joyful air, which suddenly cracked the solidified solemnity. They are so lively and free, but we humans, who claim to be the soul of all things, have lost our freedom and liveliness everywhere, and only groan and moan under the heavy pressure of pain. Thinking about it, isn't it embarrassing!

The heavy evening dew is gradually lowering, and the last ray of sunlight has been retracted from the spire of the Cathedral of the Holy Mother. Therefore, I also had to quietly embark on the road home with a wistful heart.

New Family and Hygiene

— Edited by Dr. Shen Zhaoquan

The Greatest Crisis in China Today!

— Editor

The situation China is in today is such that the severity of the crisis cannot be described in words. Externally, Eastern tigers and Western wolves, powerful neighbors are pressing in. Internally, natural disasters and banditry, everywhere is scarred and battered. It is just like a small boat drifting in the midst of terrifying waves, constantly in danger of capsizing. However, the perilous state of the country, though a great tragedy, is not the greatest affliction of our Chinese nation. Rather, the weakness of our people's bodies is the greatest crisis.

The country is a collective body of people. If the individuals that make up the country are strong in quality, then even if the organization of the country is destroyed, we still have the possibility of reorganizing it. But if the bodies of the people are weak, first there will be a loss of spirit and an apathetic attitude, followed by the onset of various diseases and a lingering existence. In such a situation, the nation's productivity will sharply decline, and the death rate will sharply increase. If this continues, then we will not be able to handle difficult tasks in the present, and we will surely perish day by day in the future.

The decline of the physique of our country's people has gradually worsened, especially in recent years. Looking at the failures of our country's representatives at the current World Games, half of them are due to a lack of physical strength. This alone is enough to give us deep attention and reflection. If we examine today's schools, there are many students who are sick. One school conducted a health check and found that the sick and unhealthy accounted for 80% of the students, while the healthy and disease-free accounted for only 20%. If the health ratio of students in all schools in the country is the same as in this school, then most of the young people are weak. Then China's future is in danger. If we extrapolate from the surface, more than half of China's 400 million people will be sick and weak. What is the danger to the nation's future?

Furthermore, when we examine the office workers in various institutions, most show signs of mental and physical decline and low vitality. Such weak people are very easily fatigued when serving, and in less than a few hours, they feel dizzy, have blurred vision, and have sore backs. Therefore, their spirits are flagging, they procrastinate in their duties, are absent from work, and their efficiency is greatly reduced. Furthermore, if we stand on the side of a thoroughfare and carefully observe the passersby, most are yellow-faced, thin, and weak. Among them, there are very few who are physically strong and mentally healthy. If this is the case, it will be truly difficult for our country, a country organized by a weak nation, to resist foreign enemies. Therefore, today's danger to China is not the fear of foreign insults, nor the worry of disasters, but the weakness of our physique, which is the greatest concern. In general, those who are mentally unhealthy will have weak wisdom and declining spirits. Therefore, the virtue of courage will also be almost completely extinguished. From this point of view, we can know the crux of the relationship between the country's strength and weakness and the nation's survival and demise.

Cultivating Health

To increase the vitality of the nerves and promote general health and vitality, the first thing is to cultivate the spirit, avoid overwork of the mind and body, have a regular life, go to bed early and wake up early, rub the body with cold water, do appropriate exercises outdoors, avoid all exciting substances, regulate bowel movements, and restrain sexual activity to prevent excess. Those who have bad habits such as masturbation should also quit. In addition, nerve tonics should also be taken at the same time to quickly recover and restore health.

Our spirit and physical strength are produced by the brain. If we want to strengthen our nerves and our physical health, we must nourish our brain. Because the brain is the hub of all nerves - if one is healthy, all are healthy; if one is weak, all are weak - so nourishing the brain is the foundation for strengthening the nerves, and it is also the key to eliminating weakness and strengthening the whole body and mind. According to the experimental reports of doctors from various countries, the "Mimer Brain Tonic" Memory Neuralic of German Keong Ke Biological Pharmaceutical Company is the most effective for such drugs that strengthen and nourish the nerves. It is effective for various symptoms of neurasthenia such as headache, brain swelling, dizziness, forgetfulness, insomnia, weak memory, sluggish thinking, and mental fatigue. After taking it, patients immediately feel clear-headed, have agile thoughts, are mentally happy, are physically strong, and have doubled vitality - as if a withered tree has gained sweet rain and grown vigorously. Therefore, doctors around the world unanimously praise "Mimer Brain Tonic" as a source of health. If the people of our country want to go from weak to strong, then taking this medicine regularly is suitable.

Record of Experiments on Rooting Out Asthma

— (British Asthma Treatment Monthly) DR.A.BERT. Report Translated by Shen Zhaoquan

Asthma, also known as bronchial asthma, is commonly called phlegm drinking. This symptom has been difficult to treat since ancient times. Although modern medicine is prosperous, there is still no effective medicine for radical cure. Most of the various asthma medicines sold in the market contain anesthetic effects, which are only effective for a while. There is actually no possibility of radical cure, and such drugs should not be used frequently. If taken every time it occurs, it will often lead to addiction, so it is not a safe treatment. I have been in clinical practice for many years. When I encounter this disease, I only use symptomatic treatment. It is extremely difficult to apply radical treatment.

Since Dr. HumbertM.D. of Germany invented the endocrine combined asthma medicine Holipin, the entire European medical community has been competing to adopt it and has published articles in magazines and newspapers to introduce it. They all praised and recognized (Xiaoli Ping) as a radical cure for asthma. Therefore, I also used it accordingly. Over the years, I have treated no less than 200 asthma patients in clinical practice, and the results have been very satisfactory. Now, in my spare time, I have extracted one example on the left.

Patient Mr. B.W., 47 years old (hardware industry)

(Chief Complaint) The body is weak and usually has a lot of phlegm. He is prone to catching a cold. Since the autumn of the year before last, he suddenly developed asthma. In the beginning, it occurred once every two or three months. Until the winter of last year, the condition worsened, and it occurred once or twice a month, and the time was prolonged, and the suffering was even greater.

(Symptoms) The onset time is often in the middle of the night. Suddenly, there is difficulty breathing. The breath is obstructed and astringent. You cannot go to bed. You have to sit or stand to relieve your breath. The face is pale and cyanotic. The snoring is like a flute sound, and the sound is very high. You can hear it if you are close. At the beginning of the attack, the cough is not very obvious. After four or five days, the difficulty breathing gradually eases. Then, there is more coughing, and thick, clear phlegm is coughed up. The symptoms are relieved and return to normal.

(Diagnosis) Bronchial asthma

(Treatment) Strictly abide by general health care methods. Take Holipin (Xiaoli Ping) three tablets at a time when it occurs. In about ten minutes, the symptoms will be relieved. Two hours later, take another three tablets, and you will feel that the phlegm is thin and loose, and the difficulty breathing will be completely returned. He then returned to a healthy state. From then on, during the intermittent period, take two tablets three times a day. After three months of continuous treatment, he was cured. And it has been more than half a year since then, and it has not recurred. From this, we can know that (Xiaoli Ping) can indeed eradicate asthma and is not false.

Lung Disease and Cough with Sputum

—The Danger of Abusing Antitussives—

What is sputum? It is the secretion from the affected area, i.e., the pus of pulmonary tuberculosis. This pus contains numerous tuberculosis bacteria (also known as tubercle bacilli). If it remains in the alveoli without being coughed out, there is a risk of further spreading the disease.

The inner lining of the trachea has ciliated epithelial cells with brush-like cilia. The movement of these cilia can naturally push out a small amount of sputum in the trachea. However, it is quite difficult to do so when there is a large amount of sputum, especially the sputum produced by the tuberculous lesion, which is very sticky. The force of the ciliary movement alone cannot completely remove it. Therefore, there must be a method to expel this sticky sputum, which is why coughing occurs. Therefore, the act of coughing is beneficial in physiologically defending against harmful sputum in the body. If it is a mild cough, it is a natural and beneficial self-defense mechanism. However, if patients abuse antitussive medications, forcibly suppressing the cough and hindering its self-defense function, it is actually harmful. Therefore, it is quite inappropriate for lung disease patients to abuse antitussive medications.

The nature of the sputum: white, thin sputum is mostly secreted from the trachea; thick, yellowish-brown sputum can be considered to be produced by the tuberculous lesion. During the recovery process, the natural reduction of sputum indicates that the pus is gradually decreasing, and the disease is gradually lessening. The change from thick sputum to thin sputum, from yellowish-brown pus to white, thin sputum, also indicates that the disease is subsiding. In general, the decrease in sputum and the disappearance of purulent sputum naturally reduce coughing, which also indicates a reduction in the disease. From this perspective, the presence of sputum in recovering patients indicates that the disease has not yet stopped. While coughing is present, it is clear that tuberculosis bacteria are still active. Thoroughly implementing rest and quiet in the air, along with internal administration of the organ-derived preparation "Phith Weal" according to the method, can quickly halt the progression of the disease. The cough can then disappear naturally without needing to be suppressed, which is the fundamental method of treatment.

Research on Germ Warfare (Part 1)

— Li Lingdong

—Special Feature on the Eve of the World War

The international situation has returned to the eve of a violent and murderous world war. The smell of gunpowder has filled the olfactory organs of people all over the world. No one dares to deny that war is inevitable. Each imperialist is flexing its muscles, scheming, and striving to expand its military power. Weapons of murder are constantly being refined day and night in order to achieve the illusion of quickly annihilating the enemy and achieving final victory.

Future wars will shift from planar warfare to three-dimensional warfare. The sharp weapons of war have evolved from bows and arrows and cruisers, etc. to places where shells arrive, causing the earth to collapse and objects to shatter. In the realm of aircraft attacks, blood and flesh fly horizontally. The cruelty and grief have reached the point where it is unbearable to hear and see. What is even more terrifying is that the imperialists are ambitious and unprincipled. The sharpness and ferocity of all killing tools make people stunned and talk about tigers as if they were changing color. Therefore, the use of brutal, inhumane, and inhuman poisonous gas warfare and germ warfare has followed one after another, shocking the world. In the blink of an eye, corpses can be seen everywhere and all the fields are destroyed. The cruelty of the murderous power makes people feel cold and frightened. Since germ warfare and poisonous gas warfare are so important in future wars, let us now take a look at germ warfare.

Although germ warfare is brutal and inhumane, it has never been used in past wars. Its first experiment was at the end of the First World War. At that time, the German army cultivated a kind of glanders bacteria in the German embassy in Bucharest, hoping to use it on the Romanian cavalry. In addition, cholera bacteria were cultivated in the Consulate General of Zurich, Switzerland, with the intention of spreading them within the Russian territory. However, before they could be used, the Russian Tsarist army had collapsed and disintegrated. The Consul General wanted to throw them into the river to destroy the evidence, but was secretly reported by the gatekeeper and discovered. This is the sensational Zurich germ bomb incident in the world, and it is also the beginning of the history of germ warfare.

Bacteria are the source of disease and the enemy of mankind. However, the bacteria used in war are mostly statutory infectious diseases, or spores that are not easily destroyed, and various pyogenic bacteria, such as cholera, typhoid fever, plague, whooping cough, cold, dysentery, tetanus, erysipelas, tuberculosis, typhus, relapsing fever, glanders bacteria, streptococcus, rabies, and the original bacteria of various pyogenic diseases.

If we want to study germ warfare, the basic approach must be to first know the morphology, living properties, and reproduction of various bacteria, as well as the methods of cultivation. On the one hand, we can manufacture sharp weapons in germ warfare to annihilate the enemy, defend the country’s territory, and realize world peace. On the other hand, if the enemy uses bacteria to attack us, we can also know how to defend against and destroy the harm of bacteria, so that germ warfare cannot show its power within our country.

The implementation of germ warfare is not an easy task. There must be suitable air pressure, temperature, and humidity for the bacteria to exert their fierce power and unfold their violence in a good environment in the air, in food, in the soil and in water. When experimenting with the transmission of cholera, if there is a good environment, the mortality rate can reach 60%, that is, 60 out of 100 people suffering from cholera are killed by cholera bacteria.

The methods of attack that various countries are expecting in germ warfare are listed below:

(1) Contamination of drinking water, such as throwing typhoid bacteria, cholera bacteria, dysentery bacteria, tuberculosis bacteria, E. coli, etc. into the drinking water. Is water something that people cannot live without for a day? Sixty percent of the body tissue is composed of water. Since the relationship between water and humans is so close, if the water contains germs, the transmission of diseases is very close, and people’s lives are in a state of "no guarantee in the morning and evening." The number of deaths is shockingly terrifying.

(2) Use rodents and other animals and insects, such as cultivating fleas, lice, bedbugs, etc., to spread germs to the enemy and drive away rabid dogs to bite people, so that plague, typhus, rabies, etc. will continue to occur.

(3) Smear tetanus bacteria, erysipelas bacteria, streptococcus, and various pyogenic bacteria on weapons or fill them in bullets and shoot them at the enemy.

(4) Store the cultured and propagated bacteria in volumetric containers, drop them from airplanes, and fill the air and drinking water with cold germs, whooping cough, and tuberculosis bacteria.

(5) Bury glanders, tetanus, and malignant edema bacteria in the mud. Once we come into contact with them, we will suffer from this disease.

From the methods of implementing germ warfare attacks, we can know that air, land, drinking water, and food...etc. are all important media that can be used in germ warfare. People can be infected with the plague and lose their lives at any time and minute. Once an infectious disease occurs, the rate of spread is very fast and the number of deaths can be astonishing. It spreads from one person, one family, one village, one township, one city, or even one province to the whole country. For example, the plague spread in the three northeastern provinces, killing as many as 100,000 people in a few hours. Cholera was prevalent in the south in the 20th year of the Republic of China, and hundreds of thousands of people died within a few months. How frightening is this high level of mortality— Once bacteria are used in germ warfare practice, the power of the plague and the cruelty of the massacre will not only harm one country, but can spread to the whole world. If plagues occur all over the world, it will be the day when mankind is exterminated and the day when the earth disappears. Therefore, it can be said that the terror of germ warfare is greater than the ferocity of poisonous gas; because the application time of poisonous gas cannot last for a long time, and the destructive power is relatively limited. The effects of poisonous gas poisoning vary, and a certain poisonous gas has a certain hazard, but not other hazards. For example, mustard gas only has the harm of corroding the skin, and tear gas can only make people shed tears, and can only be harmed in its area, and will never spread to a very distant place. Therefore, the abhorrence and fear of germ warfare is known from this. We should urgently study germ warfare.

(2) Education Level of the Populace

Narrative of Li Kejia and Li Kejia Disease (4)

— Chen Duanbai

The intracellular growth and proliferation of Li Kejia within blood vessels is an easily demonstrable fact in the course of epidemic typhus. Conversely, it is not easily demonstrable in the course of scrub typhus. The existence of Li Kejia in other cells or tissues, due to staining difficulties, still lacks a definitive method of judgment. In blood smear specimens and tissue section specimens, Li Kejia can be found, but the procedure is not easy. Based on personal experience, even with skin papules or testicular smears of experimental animals, if prepared one or two hours after the material is taken, it is difficult to stain and be detected. This shows that Li Kejia's ability to survive outside cells is extremely weak. The reason why it cannot be detected in the patient's blood may also be unrelated to this.

(6) Transmission Methods and Immunology Aspects

The transmission of various Li Kejia diseases is not directly from person to person. Instead, a middleman acts as the vector for this task. Each Li Kejia disease has its own specialized vector, listed as follows.

(1) The vector (transmitter) of epidemic typhus is the body louse Pediculus Vestimenti.

(2) The vector of scrub typhus is the scrub mite (red mite) Trombicula Akamushi.

(3) The vector of Rocky Mountain spotted fever is the wood tick Permacemtor Venustus.

(4) The vector of trench fever is lice of an undetermined type Lausenart.

In addition to the vector, there is also a long-term reservoir of the pathogen, the so-called "Vlrustregr" in this play. Non-human hosts and past patients are animals, such as wild mice, Microsus Montebelli in scrub typhus. The method of transmission is that infected lice carrying Li Kejia in their active and proliferative stages pierce the skin when sucking human blood. Because Li Kejia constantly reproduces in the digestive tract, the epithelial cells of the intestine or stomach in lice undergo unlimited reproduction, and when the cell volume is excessive and cannot hold more, it will rupture. These Li Kejia then flow into the wound along with the leakage of digestive fluids. At this location, an initial rash occurs, gradually leading to local necrosis, sometimes becoming an ulcer, and then spreading to the body and other parts. The route taken at this time, according to the facts of pathological dissection, is of course still along the outer walls of blood vessels. In addition to the pathological tissue conditions, the main point of the cause of the disease is undoubtedly the production of toxins. After one encounter with Li Kejia, so-called immunity can be obtained. In other words, a second occurrence is unlikely. However, this immunity is not absolute. There is sometimes the possibility of a second infection, but it will be easier to recover from. Although the existence of antitoxins has not yet been directly proven, skin allergic reactions were demonstrated in past epidemic typhus patients by Wantman and Brockdy Goodmann & Kroide in a report from the Department of Medical Microbiology at New York University. Regarding the skin allergic reaction of scrub typhus, the author also successfully obtained it on immune animals while staying at the Institute of Infectious Diseases in Tokyo last year (1935), and repeated trials yielded the same results. Currently, it is being tested on past scrub typhus patients. Regardless of the outcome, judging from the author's clinical and pathological facts, the existence of immunity (antitoxins) is beyond doubt. Antikorper Immunitat

(7) Clinical Symptoms

(Various Li Kejia diseases vary slightly; here, epidemic typhus is used as an example for explanation.)

The incubation period of epidemic typhus is usually four to fourteen days, rarely exceeding two weeks. At the beginning, a high fever appears, usually reaching 39 to 40 degrees Celsius or higher, slightly lower in the morning, but is a strong fever lasting two weeks to the fourteenth or fifteenth day, then drops suddenly. The period of rash production is usually the fourth to sixth day after the onset of the disease. Initially, it is irregular fine spots the size of pinheads, with the surface raised above the skin, giving a pricking sensation when touched. When pressed, the redness disappears, but after two or three days, the rash becomes more apparent, the redness deepens, and the center appears dark red, forming hemorrhagic spots. After two weeks, it begins to disappear on its own, replaced by colored spots, which gradually fade on their own as the disease heals. The initial sites of appearance are the abdomen, chest, and shoulders, gradually spreading to the whole body, with the face and neck being exceptions. Common symptoms are severe headache, back pain, nausea, and extreme fatigue. Conjunctivitis is also an early symptom, so patients are very sensitive to light. The facial skin is completely flushed, the mind is unclear, and sleep is disturbed, often suffering from insomnia.

Common Knowledge Question and Answer on Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(94) Chronic Gastric Mucositis

(Question) How does chronic gastric mucositis arise?

(Answer) The cause of this disease is either a continuation of acute gastric mucositis or, like acute gastric mucositis, it is caused by dietary carelessness. It can also be caused by excessive drinking and smoking.

(Question) When the body suffers from which diseases, will this disease be complicated?

(Answer) When suffering from liver cirrhosis, kidney disease, syphilis, tuberculosis, anemia, heart disease, respiratory disease, stomach cancer, gastric dilatation, etc., chronic gastric mucositis is mostly complicated.

(Question) What are the symptoms of chronic gastric mucositis?

(Answer) They are roughly the same as acute ones. However, the symptoms are not as acute. Patients have symptoms such as lack of appetite, fullness in the stomach, pressure in the stomach, belching, heartburn, and a thick coating on the tongue.

(Question) What are the objective symptoms?

(Answer) Pressing on the patient's stomach with the hand reveals fullness, tenderness to the touch, and a splashing sound.

(Question) How does a patient with this disease feel uncomfortable?

(Answer) Patients feel heaviness in the head, headache, insomnia, reduced work ability, mental disturbance, gastric vertigo, etc. And the overall nutritional status is naturally impaired.

(Question) Is there any abnormality in gastric secretion?

(Answer) There is a lack of free hydrochloric acid in the gastric juice, while mucus secretion increases.

(Question) How is chronic gastric mucositis diagnosed?

(Answer) It is not difficult to diagnose based on the above symptoms; however, it should be distinguished from stomach cancer, gastric neurosis, and lack of gastric juice.

(Question) What point should be emphasized in the treatment of this disease?

(Answer) In the treatment of chronic gastric mucositis, the first thing to do is to find out the cause and remove it. This is the most important point.

(Question) What attention should be paid to the patient's food?

(Answer) The patient's food must avoid oily and greasy foods, limit vegetable and fruit foods, eat more rice, flour, and sugar, and avoid drinking alcohol, spices, and excess water.

(Question) What medicines are used for the treatment of chronic gastric mucositis?

(Answer) The medicines for treating this disease are nothing more than acidic agents, bitter agents, alkaline agents, and digestive enzyme preparations.

(Question) How are acidic agents used?

(Answer) Acidic agents, commonly use dilute hydrochloric acid, and digestive enzyme pepsin is used at the same time. Aodiol Pepsin is a preparation that has already been combined.

(Question) What are the types of bitter agents?

(Answer) There are many kinds of bitter agents, such as Cendurango preparations, gentian, bitter tincture, quinine tincture, Colombo root decoction, etc. Their effects are all to promote gastric movement and secretion.

(Question) Which alkaline agents are used?

(Answer) The most common alkaline agents are sodium bicarbonate, calcined magnesia, mineral spring water, Cal-Bis Mo, magnesium peroxide, etc.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Comment

Confusing and Unpredictable European Political Situation

— Wo

The King of Belgium's announcement of neutrality the other day has greatly changed the European situation. The New York Min Sheng Jiang Tan Bao (New York People's Voice Forum Newspaper) said that the European collective security system had already died young, and this time the King of Belgium's announcement of neutrality is like giving it the final blow. Indeed, the King of Belgium did not consult with Britain and France beforehand, and the sudden announcement of this speech made Britain and France suspicious and uneasy. France and Belgium originally had a close relationship, and cooperation between France and Belgium was still difficult to contain Germany, which was full of ambition. Therefore, the Franco-Belgian alliance has long been an important factor in France's defense preparations. Now, because of Belgium's actions, the Maginot Line must be extended from the Belgian border to the coast. This has added another layer of defensive work to France, and the European situation has inevitably been shaken.

Moreover, this decision by the King to announce neutrality, from the surface, is that France has one less helper. If the King of Belgium changes his national policy and is nominally neutral but actually favors Germany, then France will not only have one less helper but also one more enemy, and the European situation would be even more unthinkable. Therefore, Britain and France are particularly suspicious, while Germany and Italy express joy. Britain and France cannot but question the true meaning of the King of Belgium's announcement of neutrality. No wonder Britain and France are deeply concerned about this move. According to European news, the King of Belgium has no intention of leaning towards Germany. His intention is nothing more than to escape the vortex of war and avoid being ravaged by airplanes and artillery. Then the suspicion that the King of Belgium favors Germany seems to be alleviated somewhat.

Belgium is to Europe like the state of Zheng was to the Spring and Autumn period, situated between two great powers, and is often subjected to the misfortunes of war. The war in Europe was a painful lesson, and it is still chilling to think about. Now, Germany is rearming and has a great determination to avenge its humiliation, and the Italian and German fascists are also reconnecting with each other. Germany and Austria also express friendship. The situation before the Great War has returned. If war breaks out again, not only Belgium would be unthinkable, but all of Europe would suffer catastrophe. However, the attitude of Britain and France is extremely soft. If Germany still follows General Schlieffen's plan before the war in Europe (i.e., passing through Belgium) to attack France, then Belgium will inevitably bear the brunt and suffer first.

Even if Germany has no intention of attacking France, and the recent Franco-Russian pact is successful, if war breaks out between Russia and Germany, then Belgium will inevitably become a battlefield for the two countries. Therefore, the reason why the King of Belgium announced strict neutrality this time is because of this. In fact, due to Belgium's geographical location, if war does not break out in Europe, that's one thing, but if war does break out, Belgium's desire to strictly adhere to neutrality is not only impossible but also beyond its ability. A country that can defend itself and is not afraid of invasion must also have great power to help others fight, the so-called "having a decisive influence." Therefore, there are still doubts about Belgium's power.

Therefore, this time the King of Belgium's announcement of neutrality greatly alarmed Britain and France and pleased Germany and Italy. But in the world, there are no coincidences. The compromise between Germany and Austria has already been successful, and the situation of the three countries (Germany, Austria, and Italy) being united seems to be settled. Unexpectedly, yesterday's newspaper reported that Austrian Chancellor Kurt Schuschnigg also issued a declaration, saying that he would maintain national independence, and that no other country should interfere in internal affairs. The political system will be decided by the people. He expressed disappointment with the Austro-German agreement. This declaration is like throwing a bomb at the German fascists. Therefore, the declarations of neutrality by Belgium and Austria can be said to offset and cancel each other out. This matter should also be welcomed by Britain and France and alarmed by Germany and Italy.

Blacksmith Lao Liu

— Lin Ji

How quickly did the life of Blacksmith Lao Liu, filled with humiliation, pass—just like an arrow leaving the string, shot out in an instant, he was already over fifty years old.

Thin as a monkey, his back had hunched over since who knows when, always with those sharp eyes open, Lao Liu's appearance was very pitiful. So old, yet he had to forge iron all day long, using those dry firewood-like arms to raise the iron hammer and strike it again and again on the red-hot iron piece. The fire in the furnace burned fiercely, right next to Lao Liu, so soon Lao Liu would sweat, dripping on the black, stagnant floor like small raindrops. In the narrow and dark blacksmith shop, the air was terribly turbid; Lao Liu, who had been breathing in such air for more than twenty years, now suffered from severe tuberculosis, coughing constantly. Spitting had become a very bad habit of his; he always spat here and there, piles of it, hygiene was not something Lao Liu like people could take into consideration, to spit a mouthful, what was it to him! Helping Lao Liu work every day were two apprentices; the smaller one squatted in a corner pulling the bellows, his face covered in black ash, a child who had just run away from the countryside not long ago. The other one used tongs to clamp out the red-hot iron block and forged it with Lao Liu—the shop resounded with the sound of "ding da… ding da" all day long.

Now, Lao Liu was all alone, without a wife, children, or relatives, truly a desolate old age. When someone asked about him, he would always lower his head, as if he had some sad thing, and silently walk away with tears in his eyes. He didn't seem to feel excited about life; but he was always a little unwilling to die—to be able to live one day with this heaven-given life, Lao Liu was satisfied enough.

I had known Lao Liu and his blacksmith shop since I was a child: later I left my hometown, year after year, my memory had faded so much that I couldn't even remember Lao Liu's face. This time I returned to my hometown, a hometown where everything had changed, and in the midst of overwhelming emotion, I happened to pass by Lao Liu's place one day and greeted him, and unexpectedly he kept me there.

It was an evening when summer was about to pass, the weather was still very hot, and Lao Liu was cooling off at the door. He told the little apprentice to carry out a bamboo chair, specially wiped off the dust on it with a cloth, and courteously invited me to sit down. I had never seen Blacksmith Lao Liu greet me so happily, I was a little strange but after a while I understood, Lao Liu's life for so many years had been too lonely, too dull, without even one person to talk to. Really, that evening he asked me many questions, about the outside world, and I answered him in detail. Lao Liu had once drifted to cities outside when he was young, but the situation now had become too difficult. In this ancient and peaceful countryside, he had stayed for more than twenty years, watching the younger generation grow up, his feelings were so deep.

"If it hadn't been for the war in the countryside that year, I would still have a home," Lao Liu suddenly brought up his past. "I remember very clearly, that year my son was already four years old, he had just learned to speak, he was smart and strong... but the artillery fire started; the Chinese were fighting fiercely for territory among themselves, so fiercely that there was no time to escape, the army窜 (cuan, meaning to flee in disorder) through this village, raped my wife, and that strong child died from excessive fear! ... So many years have passed since this happened, and I haven't forgotten it at all!" Speaking of this, tears flowed from the corners of his sharp eyes, and he also looked up and sighed deeply.

I had never known about Blacksmith Lao Liu's tragedy before. Since then, he no longer had a close person, and silently carried the burden of life, limping along on the journey of life. Now, Lao Liu was aging.

I didn't know how to comfort him, thinking about how the civil war had destroyed his happiness, and the whip of life had hunched his back, and I couldn't help but sigh.

When autumn came, I left the ancient hometown again and drifted outside. Every time I thought of my hometown, I remembered the conversation I had with Blacksmith Lao Liu that night. I thought he must still be silently holding the iron hammer, hitting the red-hot iron block, passing the days of his old age.

Autumn Night

— Yan Ting

Walking along the river ferry, I arrived at the beach.

The moonlight was hazy, the tide had already receded, and the beach had become wide and quiet. The noise of this city disappeared on the other side of the gray-white city wall. There was no human sound here, and I couldn't hear the galloping of cars and horses, and the shouting. There was only gloom and emptiness.

I strolled on the sand, my eyes looking at the distant village, where the weak howls of dogs often came from, listening quietly to the groaning of the seabed; but these could not fill the dryness and emptiness in my heart. Three days ago, I came to this small city with a stomach full of hope, and three days later, I sold all my things and was starving. So wandering on this beach every night has become a daily life course for me.

Gently I strolled from this side to that side, and then wanted to stroll from that side to this side, but a short and strange sound attracted me. I hesitated and stood still, locking in the surroundings. I couldn't see anything, there was only the sound of the night wind hitting the banyan tree branches on the shore, and the groaning of the seabed. So I lifted my feet again and wanted to continue the endless wandering, but I didn't continue for some time. In that deathly silence, I heard a sob, coming from a ruined temple on the shore. I began to walk over there.

This was a dilapidated temple, the palace pavilion had collapsed, the stone courtyard was covered with broken tiles and remnants of gray soil, piled up into a small hill, with centipede grass growing on it. The temple was very dark, filled with a musty and damp smell. I stepped onto the stone steps of the palace pavilion and suddenly stopped. The sobs became clearer, coming from people's throats, and from a woman's throat.

I began to pay attention to every corner of this temple. In the place where good men and women worshiped, I found a clump, small, grayish-white animal wriggling, moving as if a wounded beast was shivering. So I coughed softly and stepped inside.

Now, I stood in front of this wriggling animal, able to see clearly its outline and every small twitch. Her head, with long hair, was being embraced by two small, naked arms, her whole body also naked and curled up. She seemed to have heard the sound of my footsteps coming in, and slowly raised her head from her arms, looking at me in surprise with big round eyes. From her small face, I determined that she was a little girl who had not yet reached maturity.

She looked at me fearfully, suddenly raised her head, and shouted loudly:

"Get out! You shameless rogue!" She lowered her head and sobbed again.

This made me so surprised that I hurriedly moved back a few steps. But she did not scare me. I mustered up the courage and ran up.

"You have already ravaged me and robbed me of everything, are you still not satisfied?" She cried for a while, as if she felt something was wrong, and raised her head again, shouting in an angry and sad tone.

"I don't understand what you mean." I also whispered in reply.

She was obviously a little surprised, because in the darkness I saw her eyes widened beyond normal.

"Who are you?" she asked doubtfully.

"Me?" I replied coldly "An unemployed man and a wanderer...

"Then what are you doing here, not with them? ..."

"What are you saying, I don't understand a word." I shook my head.

"Maybe you're not with them." She muttered to herself "Just now two big men were here and ×× me, and before leaving they stripped the clothes off my body...

"Who are you? You said people ×× you. ..."

"Me?" she said coldly with a laugh, "A prostitute..." Then lowed her voice to add: "In the evening I sing songs for a few customers in a teahouse, and two big men asked me to go to a hotel with them, so I went with them, but they didn't go to a hotel, they cheated me to come here. ..."

"Where are they now!"

"They didn't give me any money, and instead snatched my clothes and ran away." Her tone became choked with sobs. "Now I have nothing, my whole body is naked, how can I go back... "She cried sadly.

I stood there blankly, a feeling of悲怆 (beichuang, sorrow) pierced me, so I took off the only set of clothes I had on my back that I used to change into and handed it to her:

"Take it, this is my last set of clothes.

After saying that, I walked out silently, facing the misty

Miscellaneous (Continued)

— Shen Shen

Everyone has the same conviction that our path is correct and the future is bright.

No one speaks, no one dares to think. Only silently walking with heads lowered, our footsteps are uniform. Thud, thud—thud, thud—thud…

What a terrifying silence—cherishing a sliver of hope: that everyone will sing a song.

But everyone didn’t sing. Yet—

Caw——a flock of crows took flight. Feeling a bit stifled, I cursed something even I couldn’t hear, as if my lips only twitched.

A bolt from the blue on a clear day, old Qu’s mouth twitched:

“Only sixty li from Fenghuang Prefectural City—li, eh…”

Ah——Heaven—is this our guide, old Qu?

Everyone was stunned. Sixty li! It seemed our ears hadn’t deceived us.

The footsteps went thud—thud—thud… slowing down. And then—

No one issued a command, but everyone stopped and sat down.

Heaven, I don’t know what time it was, but it was getting dark. A few stars reflected in squinting eyes, looking just like those of devils, damn it!

The round moon was embedded in the gray-green sky, hanging above our heads. Frost-like moonlight sprinkled on the land with tall sorghum, on the hills covered with trees, and also on the faces of this group of desperate men. It was so fair, so gentle.

Lovely moon!

Three. Silence. Yet silence accomplishes nothing. We must continue, we must endure, according to our agreement.

Our agreement: We agreed to disband sixty li from the prefectural city. We have reached a dead end, receiving no supplies, and surrounded by large numbers of devil soldiers. Our own strength is small, and our bullets are pitifully few. Now there is nothing we can do but leave behind eleven hardened men. We have other important missions to carry out! Now—

After giving the five brothers and the brothers from other units one last farewell, then we eleven…

Go! We leave. Tears are flowing, hoarse throats are shouting.

“Farewell, brothers! Take care. Someday, we will meet again!”

Tears blurred my eyes. Old Li, the tall one!… each one flashed before me, nodding.

My heart aches. Finally, I left them, and they left me. Alone, I set foot on the frosty, moonlit road.

Wave after wave of the unique, cool fragrance of the sorghum fields of Guanwai hits me!
